### [41] [Systematic Biases in Gravitational-Wave Parameter Estimation from Neglecting Orbital Eccentricity in Space-Based Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07739)
*Jin-Zhao Yang,Jia-Hao Zhong,Tao Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了在分析具有轨道偏心率的致密双星并合信号时，使用准圆形波形模板所导致的参数估计偏差。研究聚焦于B-DECIGO（分赫兹）和LISA（毫赫兹）空间引力波探测器，发现即使极小的初始偏心率（如B-DECIGO中e₀~10⁻⁴–10⁻³）也会引起显著系统偏差，因此未来空间探测需在波形模型中纳入偏心率效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确建模引力波信号对可靠推断致密双星源参数至关重要，尤其对工作在毫赫兹和分赫兹频段的未来空间探测器；而现有准圆波形模板忽略轨道偏心率，可能导致显著系统偏差。

Method: 采用包含偏心率诱导高次谐波及空间探测器时变响应的频域波形模型，结合贝叶斯推断与Fisher-Cutler-Vallisneri（FCV）形式，量化啁啾质量、对称质量比和光度距离的系统偏差，并通过构建覆盖恒星级与大质量黑洞双星的模拟引力波星表确定临界初始偏心率。

Result: B-DECIGO在0.1 Hz处仅需e₀~10⁻⁴–10⁻³即可引发显著偏差；LISA则需更高偏心率（e₀~10⁻²–10⁻¹，对应10⁻⁴ Hz），因其频带内周期数更少；FCV预测与贝叶斯分析在波形失配较小时高度一致。

Conclusion: 未来空间引力波观测必须在波形模型中纳入轨道偏心率，否则将导致不可忽视的参数估计系统偏差。

Abstract: Accurate modeling of gravitational-wave signals is essential for reliable inference of compact-binary source parameters, particularly for future space-based detectors operating in the milli- and deci-Hertz bands. In this work, we systematically investigate the parameter-estimation biases induced by neglecting orbital eccentricity when analyzing eccentric compact-binary coalescences with quasi-circular waveform templates. Focusing on the deci-Hertz detector B-DECIGO and the milli-Hertz detector LISA, we model eccentric inspiral signals using a frequency-domain waveform that incorporates eccentricity-induced higher harmonics and the time-dependent response of spaceborne detectors. We quantify systematic biases in the chirp mass, symmetric mass ratio, and luminosity distance using both Bayesian inference and the Fisher-Cutler-Vallisneri (FCV) formalism, and assess their significance relative to statistical uncertainties. By constructing mock gravitational-wave catalogs spanning stellar-mass and massive black-hole binaries, we identify critical initial eccentricities at which systematic errors become comparable to statistical errors. We find that for B-DECIGO, even very small eccentricities, $e_0\sim 10^{-4}-10^{-3}$ at 0.1 Hz, can lead to significant biases, whereas for LISA such effects typically arise at larger eccentricities, $e_0\sim 10^{-2}-10^{-1}$ at $10^{-4}$ Hz, due to the smaller number of in-band cycles. Comparisons between FCV predictions and full Bayesian analyses demonstrate good agreement within the regime where waveform mismatches remain small, especially when extrinsic parameters are pre-aligned to minimize mismatches. Our results highlight the necessity of incorporating eccentricity in waveform models for future space-based gravitational-wave observations.

### [42] [Boundary-only weak deflection angles from isothermal optical geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06864)
*Ali Övgün,Reggie C. Pantig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种仅依赖边界的弱引力偏转角计算方法，基于高斯-博内定理和光学几何，在等温坐标下将曲率积分转化为纯边界贡献，从而避免轨道依赖的校准，适用于有限距离源与观测者情形，并在Schwarzschild、Reissner-Nordström和Kottler时空等案例中验证了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统引力透镜偏转角计算常依赖于完整测地线积分或渐近平坦假设，难以处理有限距离源/接收器及非渐近平坦时空（如含宇宙常数情形）；本文旨在建立一种更普适、几何本质更清晰、仅需边界数据的计算框架。

Method: 基于光学几何的二维赤道面，引入等温（共形）坐标，使光学度规局部共形于平直参考度规；利用高斯曲率可表为共形因子拉普拉斯的性质，通过格林/斯托克斯型关系将高斯-博内定理中的曲率面积分转化为纯边界积分；保留共形半径归一化自由度并证明其不影响物理观测量。

Result: 导出了仅依赖边界数据和可控闭合项的弱场偏转角公式；在弱场近似下，主阶偏转简化为共形平面上沿直线路径的一维积分，有限距离效应仅体现在端点数据中；成功复现Schwarzschild时空有限距离结果，首次给出Reissner-Nordström电荷修正的主阶项，并在Kottler（Schwarzschild-de Sitter）时空中完整重现含Λ及ΛM混合项的有限距离偏转展开。

Conclusion: 该边界仅方法提供了一种几何直观、计算简洁且普适性强的新范式，摆脱了对完整测地线求解和渐近条件的依赖，为复杂时空（尤其含宇宙常数或电荷）下的引力透镜研究提供了统一工具。

Abstract: We develop a boundary only method for computing weak gravitational deflection angles at finite source and receiver distances within the Gauss-Bonnet theorem formulation of optical geometry. Exploiting the fact that the relevant equatorial optical manifold is two dimensional, we introduce isothermal (conformal) coordinates in which the optical metric is locally conformal to a flat reference metric and the Gaussian curvature reduces to a Laplacian of the conformal factor. Such an identity converts the curvature area term in the Gauss-Bonnet theorem into a pure boundary contribution via Green/Stokes-type relations, yielding a deflection formula that depends only on boundary data and controlled closure terms. The residual normalization freedom of the isothermal radius is isolated as an additive freedom in the conformal factor and is shown to leave physical observables invariant, eliminating the need for orbit dependent calibration prescriptions. We explicitly implement the boundary only formalism in weak deflection, where the leading bending reduces to elementary one-dimensional integrals evaluated on a flat reference ray in the conformal plane, with finite distance dependence entering solely through endpoint data. We validate the construction by reproducing finite distance weak deflection for Schwarzschild, deriving the leading finite distance charge correction for Reissner-Nordström, and applying the same boundary only framework to the Kottler (Schwarzschild-de Sitter) geometry as a representative non-asymptotically flat test case, recovering the standard finite distance expansion including the explicit $\mathcal{O}(Λ)$ and mixed $\mathcal{O}(ΛM)$ contributions to the total deflection angle.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The solution space of differentially rotating polytropes with n=1 has been studied numerically. The existence of three different types of configurations: from spheroids to thick tori, hockey puck-like bodies and spheroids surrounded by a torus, separate from or merging with the central body has been proved. It has been shown that the last two types appear only at moderate degrees of rotation differentiality, sigma~2. Rigid-body or weakly differential rotation, as well as strongly differential, have not led to any "exotic" types of configurations. Many calculated configurations have had extremely large values of parameter tau, which has raised the question of their stability with respect to fragmentation.

Abstract: Two $F(R)$ gravity models are tested on the basis of their viability during all stages of cosmological evolution. It is shown that these models can describe both the early-time inflationary epoch and the dark energy epoch. Investigation of the viability conditions for these models, in particular, the condition $\frac{dF}{dR}>0$ required a deep analysis. Both models appeared to be viable during the early-time era, but for the late-time evolution the viability conditions are not fulfilled in definite domains in the parameter spaces of these models. However the best fitted parameters, determined in confrontation with the mentioned observational data, lie far from the forbidden domains for both models. These $F(R)$ gravity models describe the observations with the large advantage over the $Λ$-Cold-Dark-Matter model, not only in $χ^2$ statistics, but also with Akaike and Bayesian information criteria. This success of the two $F(R)$ gravity scenarios is connected with their capability to mimic dynamical dark energy, similarly to models with variable equation of state, that is necessary for describing the latest Pantheon+ and DESI observational data.

Method: 基于三航天器L型空间干涉仪构型（臂长1000 km，日心轨道），建模轨道运动与天线响应；采用IndIGO-D合作组提供的标称灵敏度曲线，计算不同引力波源的可观测红移距离；开展贝叶斯参数估计模拟（以GW170817类事件为例），评估随时间演化的天空定位精度。

Result: 中等质量黑洞并合（10²–10³ M⊙）可达z ∼ 10³；双中子星并合可达z ≲ 0.3，实现与Voyager级地面探测器的连续多频段覆盖；GW170817类事件的定位精度在并合前6小时达0.3 deg²，可被Rubin天文台高效覆盖；具备从数月到数小时量级的早期预警能力。

Conclusion: IndIGO-D有望成为连接空间与地面引力波探测的关键桥梁，显著推动多波段引力波天文学与多信使天体物理学的发展。

Abstract: We study IndIGO-D, a decihertz gravitational-wave mission concept, focusing on a specific configuration in which three spacecraft fly in formation to form an L-shaped interferometer in a heliocentric orbit. The two orthogonal arms share a common vertex, providing a space-based analogue of terrestrial Michelson detectors, while operating in an optimised configuration that yields ppm-level arm-length stability. Assuming 1000 km arm length, we analyse the orbital motion and antenna response, and assess sensitivity across the [0.1 - 10] Hz band bridging LISA and next-generation ground-based interferometers. Using fiducial sensitivity curves provided by the IndIGO-D collaboration, we compute horizon distances for different source classes. Intermediate-mass black-hole binaries with masses $10^{2}$ - $10^{3} \, M_\odot$ are detectable to redshifts $z \sim 10^{3}$, complementing the reach of LISA and terrestrial detectors. Binary neutron star systems are observable to a horizon distance of $z \lesssim 0.3$, allowing continuous multi-band coverage with Voyager-class interferometers from the decihertz regime to merger. A Bayesian parameter-estimation study of a GW170817-like binary shows that the sky localization area improves from $\sim 21 \,\mathrm{deg}^2$ at one month to $0.3 \,\mathrm{deg}^2$ at six hours pre-merger! These sky areas are readily tiled by wide-field time-domain telescopes such as the Rubin Observatory, whose $9.6 \,\mathrm{deg}^2$ field of view and r-band depth enable high-cadence, repeated coverage of GW170817-like kilonovae at this distance and beyond. IndIGO-D exploits the rapid evolution of binaries in the decihertz band to bridge the gap between millihertz and terrestrial observations, enabling early warnings on timescales from months to hours and enhancing the prospects for multi-band and multi-messenger discoveries.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为经典Kasner解的稳定性提供更简洁、更具结构性的新证明，同时拓展适用于极化U(1)对称情形下的分析框架。

Method: (2+1)正交标架分解、精细对称化处理、将爱因斯坦真空方程约化为Fuchsian系统与约束方程耦合系统，并利用Fuchsian理论及约束传播有限速性进行分析。

Result: 在极化U(1)对称下，扰动解渐近逐点趋于Kasner形式，具有测地不完备性，并在大爆炸奇点处发生挤压（crushing）；获得了奇点前全局解的存在性与精确渐近结构。

Conclusion: 该新方法不仅复现了原有稳定性结论，还揭示了对称性在奇点附近动力学中的关键作用，为更一般时空奇点的稳定性研究提供了可推广的技术路径。

Abstract: In this paper, we give a new proof to a past stability result established in Fournodavlos-Rodnianski-Speck (arXiv:2012.05888), for Kasner solutions of the $(3+1)$-dimensional Einstein vacuum equations under polarized $U(1)$-symmetry. Our method, inspired by Beyer-Oliynyk-Olvera-Santamar{\'ı}a-Zheng (arXiv:1907.04071, arXiv:2502.09210), relies on a newly developed $(2+1)$ orthonormal-frame decomposition and a careful symmetrization argument, after which the Fuchsian techniques can be applied.
  We show that the perturbed solutions are asymptotically pointwise Kasner, geodesically incomplete and crushing at the Big Bang singularity. They are achieved by reducing the $(3+1)$ Einstein vacuum equations to a Fuchsian system coupled with several constraint equations, with the symmetry assumption playing an important role in the reduction. Using Fuchsian theory together with finite speed of constraints propagation, we obtain global existence and precise asymptotics of the solutions up to the singularities.

### [49] [Spacetime Quasi-normal Mode Oscillations of Anisotropic Neutron Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06962)
*Jihao Yu,Victor Guedes,Shu Yan Lau,Siddarth Ajith,Kent Yagi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次计算了具有压力各向异性的中子星的时空振荡模式（w模），发现随着切向压力相对于径向压力增强，w模频率的实部和虚部均减小；在物理允许参数范围内未发现不稳定w模，但在非物理解中出现；w模实部与星体致密性呈准普适关系，而虚部则依赖于各向异性程度但对物态方程普适。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星内部压力通常被假定为各向同性，但弹性、粘滞、磁场等机制可能导致压力各向异性；已有研究集中于流体模，而时空模（w模）在各向异性情况下的行为尚属空白。

Method: 采用作者先前发展的、适用于压力各向异性的恒星振荡微扰理论框架，并结合一个唯象各向异性模型，首次计算各向异性中子星的w-mode振荡频率。

Result: 1) w-mode频率实部与虚部均随切向压力相对增强而减小；2) 物理参数范围内无不稳定w-mode，但非物理解中出现；3) 实部-致密性关系具准普适性（不依赖物态方程与各向异性程度），虚部-致密性关系依赖各向异性程度但固定各向异性时对物态方程普适；4) 讨论了可能的模交叉及各向同性情形下有效近似在各向异性下的适用性。

Conclusion: 压力各向异性显著影响中子星w-mode特性，其频率演化规律揭示了新的普适性与依赖性特征，为利用引力波观测约束中子星内部各向异性及核物质性质提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Neutron star asteroseismology offers a unique opportunity to probe nuclear physics through stellar oscillations. Although the pressure inside of a neutron star is typically assumed to be isotropic, pressure anisotropy can arise from various physical mechanisms, including elasticity, viscosity, and magnetic fields. Previous studies of nonradial stellar quasi-normal mode oscillations with anisotropic pressure have focused primarily on fluid modes. In this paper, we compute, for the first time, spacetime oscillation modes (so-called w-modes) of anisotropic neutron stars. Using a perturbative framework for stellar oscillations with pressure anisotropy, developed previously by some of the authors, together with a phenomenological anisotropy model, we find that both the real and imaginary parts of the w-mode frequencies decrease as the tangential pressure becomes dominant over the radial pressure. Although we do not find any unstable w-modes within the physically viable parameter space, unstable w-modes appear in an unphysical branch of solutions when the tangential pressure strongly dominates the radial one. We also find that the relation between the real part of the w-mode frequency and the stellar compactness is quasi-universal with respect to variations in the equation of state and the degree of pressure anisotropy. In contrast, the relation between the imaginary part of the w-mode frequency and the stellar compactness depends on the degree of anisotropy, but remains equation-of-state universal when the anisotropy is fixed. Finally, we discuss potential mode crossings and the validity of certain approximations that have been shown to work well for w-mode calculations in the isotropic case.

Method: 构建依赖H、\dot H和\ddot H的红外截断的广义全息暗能量模型；分析其背景动力学，重点研究欠阻尼情形下的哈勃参数振荡衰减行为；将完整非线性背景演化与宇宙钟（cosmic chronometer）观测数据进行拟合检验。

Result: 模型导出渐进停止的宇宙膨胀解：H指数衰减至零，尺度因子有限增长，曲率不变量指数衰减，最终达渐近闵氏时空；与观测数据拟合优度高（χ²/ν ≈ 0.52）；可观测红移范围内振荡特征被强烈压制，符合现有约束。

Abstract: We study a generalized holographic dark energy model in which the infrared cutoff depends on the Hubble parameter and its first two time derivatives. The inclusion of the $\ddot H$ term introduces a finite relaxation timescale for the horizon degrees of freedom, which can be interpreted as an effective entropic inertia of the holographic vacuum energy. The resulting background dynamics admit late--time solutions in which the cosmic expansion gradually halts.
  In the underdamped regime, the Hubble parameter undergoes exponentially damped oscillations and asymptotically approaches $H\to0$. The scale factor grows monotonically but by a finite amount, while curvature invariants decay exponentially, leading to an asymptotically Minkowski spacetime without future singularities. We confront the full nonlinear background evolution with cosmic chronometer measurements of the Hubble parameter and find good agreement with current late--time expansion data, with a reduced chi--squared $χ^2/ν\simeq0.52$. At observable redshifts, oscillatory features are strongly suppressed and remain consistent with existing constraints.

### [51] [Balance flux laws beyond general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07091)

Main category: gr-qc

Method: 采用Wald-Zoupas协变相空间形式主义定义守恒量，针对一类Horndeski理论推导零无穷处通量表达式及对应平衡方程；通过与Brans-Dicke理论已有结果比对验证，并拓展至更广微分同胚不变理论；最后与Isaacson引力辐射方法所得零记忆通量进行比较验证。

Result: 得到了Horndeski类理论中零无穷处通量的一般表达式和相应平衡方程；验证了其在Brans-Dicke理论中的正确性；证实该方法可推广；零记忆相关通量部分与Isaacson方法一致。

Conclusion: Wald-Zoupas协变相空间方法可系统应用于各类微分同胚不变引力理论以构建通量平衡律，为高精度引力波数据分析和广义相对论偏差检验提供了普适框架，并促进了Isaacson方法与协变相空间形式主义之间的理论统一。

Abstract: Balance flux laws of asymptotic symmetries in general relativity provide fully non-perturbative constraint equations on gravitational strain. They have proven useful for constructing numerical gravitational waveforms and for characterizing gravitational memory. As the precision of current and future detectors continues to improve, such constraints become increasingly important for high-precision tests of gravity, including searches for deviations from general relativity. This motivates a systematic understanding of analogous balance laws in theories beyond general relativity. In this work, we investigate the existence and structure of flux laws at null infinity in diffeomorphism-invariant extensions of general relativity. Our analysis is based on the covariant phase space formalism and the definition of conserved quantities, as presented by Wald and Zoupas. For a particularly relevant class of Horndeski theories, we derive a general expression for the flux and formulate the corresponding balance equation via the associated non-conserved charges. We cross-check our general results by comparing them with previous studies of Brans-Dicke gravity. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the employed methods extend straightforwardly to a broader class of diffeomorphism-invariant theories. The null part of the resulting flux laws associated with null memory is compared with and validated against the alternative derivation based on the Isaacson approach to gravitational radiation. Beyond the specific results obtained, this work is intended to serve as a practical guide for computing balance laws in generic diffeomorphism-invariant theories of gravity and paves the way for an in-depth comparison between the Isaacson approach and the covariant phase space formalism.

*A. A. Araújo Filho,K. E. L. de Farias,E. Passos,F. A. Brito,Ali Övgün,Hassan Hassanabadi,V. B. Bezerra,Amilcar R. Queiroz*

Method: 基于光学-力学对应原理推导含洛伦兹破缺参数λ的修正色散关系；据此计算有效折射率、群速度、时间延迟、两体势与电子散射截面；构建基于变形能动关系的统计系综，解析求解热力学量；并正则化计算弯曲时空中的卡西米尔能量。

Abstract: We investigate how spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking in bumblebee gravity modifies particle dynamics, thermodynamics, and vacuum energy around a static black hole background. Starting from the optical-mechanical correspondence, we derive a modified dispersion relation that encodes the influence of the Lorentz-violating parameter $λ$ on the propagation of massive and massless modes. We analyze the resulting optical properties, including the effective refractive index, group velocity, and energy-dependent time delay, and show how the non-asymptotically flat geometry reshapes signal propagation. From the same dispersion relation, we construct the interparticle potential for massive and massless excitations and evaluate the electron scattering cross section within the Born approximation, identifying characteristic Lorentz-violating corrections. We then develop a statistical-ensemble description based on the deformed energy-momentum relation and obtain analytic expressions for the thermodynamic observables of a massless bosonic gas. The pressure, mean energy, entropy, and heat capacity are examined in three representative regimes--extremely close to the horizon, near the photon sphere, and in the asymptotic region -- where Lorentz violation systematically increase the magnitude of these quantities and leads to finite asymptotic plateaus. Finally, we analyze the vacuum state in the curved background and compute the regularized Casimir energy at zero and finite temperature.

Abstract: We propose the gravitational analog of the chiroptical effect for the first time, demonstrating that gravitational waves (GWs) can induce a reversal of photon chirality through the exchange of angular momentum, namely the spin-2-gravitation chiroptical effect. By analyzing the interaction between photon spin angular momentum (SAM) and GWs, we derive the selection rules governing this exchange, which are strictly dictated by the spin-1 and spin-2 nature of the electromagnetic and gravitational fields, respectively. We find that the gravitational chiroptical effect reflects the local nature of SAM which prevents the accumulation of gravitational perturbations over spatial phase windings, and offers a theoretically rigorous tool to probe the chiral structure of GWs. This mechanism provides a novel observational pathway to constrain modified gravity theories, measure the asymmetric properties of compact binaries, and explore parity-violating physics in the early universe.

  <summary>Details</summary>

These solutions are typically obtained under the assumption that the vector-field potential vanishes everywhere once the vector field acquires a nonzero radial vacuum expectation value. However, imposing this assumption globally obstructs the construction of self-consistent compact-star solutions. In this work, we elucidate the origin of this inconsistency through a detailed analysis of the field equations and construct neutron-star configurations by abandoning the global vanishing-potential assumption. Crucially, we show that even without enforcing this condition everywhere, it is violated only in the strong-field interior region and is dynamically restored in the weak-field regime by asymptotic boundary conditions at spatial infinity. ### [55] [A universal lower bound on the photon sphere radius in higher-dimensional black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07289)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该结果将Hod定理推广至高维，为扩展引力理论中黑洞结构提供了新的普适几何约束。

Abstract: The photon sphere, a hypersurface of circular null geodesics, plays a fundamental role in characterizing black hole spacetimes, influencing phenomena such as black hole shadows, gravitational lensing, and quasinormal modes. While universal upper bounds on the photon sphere radius have been established for both four-dimensional and higher-dimensional black holes, the question of a corresponding lower bound in higher-dimensional black holes remains less explored. In this work, we derive a universal lower bound for the photon sphere radius in static, spherically symmetric, asymptotically flat black hole spacetimes of arbitrary dimension $n\ge 4$. Under the assumptions of the weak energy condition, a non-positive trace of the energy-momentum tensor, and a monotonicity condition on the radial pressure function $|r^{n-1}p_r(r)|$, we prove that the photon sphere radius $r_γ$ satisfies $r_γ\ge (\frac{n-1}{2})^{1/(n-3)}r_H$, where $r_H$ is the radius of the outer event horizon. For $n=4$, this reduces to the known result $r_γ\ge \frac{3}{2}r_H$. Our result generalizes Hod's four-dimensional theorem to higher dimensions, and provides a new geometric constraint on the structure of black holes in extended theories of gravity.

</details>


### [56] [Superspace worldline formalism approach to Quantum Gravity: dimensional reduction and Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07382)
*Jean-Baptiste Roux*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用ADM形式主义，将量子引力的哈密顿表述转化为超空间中的世界线形式，并通过Keldysh路径积分揭示其与三维欧氏引力及二维共形场论的深刻联系，同时结合Chern-Simons/Liouville对应计算了宇宙学边界上虚引力子交换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子引力在哈密顿框架下的结构本质，建立其与已知量子场论（如CFT）和拓扑引力（如Chern-Simons理论）之间的桥梁，并理解时间参数在量子宇宙学中的物理含义。

Method: 采用ADM分解构建量子引力的哈密顿形式；运用Keldysh闭合时间路径方法构造非平衡配分函数；在规范场表述下分析其与2D CFT生成泛函的对应；借助Chern-Simons/Liouville对偶性计算边界上的虚引力子传播。

Result: 1) 量子引力哈密顿系统等价于超空间中的世界线理论；2) Keldysh配分函数约化为三维欧氏引力配分函数；3) 在规范场表述中导出具有最小时间间隔（∝√Λ）的2D CFT生成泛函；4) 计算得到宇宙学边界上两质量探针间虚引力子交换的可观测量。

Conclusion: 量子引力在特定表述下展现出强约束的几何与代数结构，其动力学可编码于低维共形理论中，且时间本身可能具有由宇宙学常数决定的微观尺度限制。

Abstract: Using the ADM formalism, we demonstrate that the Hamiltonian formulation of Quantum Gravity is exactly in the form of a worldline (WL) formalism in the superspace. We then show that the Keldysh partition function reduces to the partition function of Euclidean 3D gravity. After discussing the meaning of the time parameter, we show that in the gauge fields formalism, our Keldysh partition function reduces to a generating functional of a 2D Conformal Field Theory (CFT). This functional exhibits a minimal time-lapse proportional to the square root of the cosmological constant. From the viewpoint of the Chern-Simons/Liouville correspondence, we calculate the exchange of virtual gravitons between two massive probes from the cosmological boundary.

</details>


### [57] [Gravitational Collapse and Singularity Formation in Brans-Dicke Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07488)
*Ayush Bidlan,Dipanjan Dey,Parth Bambhaniya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了仅由自相互作用Brans-Dicke标量场驱动的引力坍缩，发现其可形成全局可见的中心曲率奇点，挑战宇宙监督假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在无普通物质情况下，仅由自相互作用Brans-Dicke标量场驱动的引力坍缩能否产生可观测的裸奇点，从而检验宇宙监督猜想。

Method: 基于Brans-Dicke理论构建标量场非最小耦合模型，数值求解标量场Φ(t)及其势能V(Φ)的演化，分析能量密度ρ≈1/a和ρ≈−ln a情形下的坍缩动力学、奇点因果结构及Tipler强曲率条件。

Result: 坍缩必然形成满足弱能条件的中心曲率奇点；该奇点全局可见（未来指向类光测地线可到达未来零无穷远）；扩展Tipler条件表明奇点具有强曲率性质。

Conclusion: 标量-张量引力中的标量场驱动坍缩可产生挑战宇宙监督猜想的裸奇点，具有潜在观测意义。

Abstract: We investigate gravitational collapse driven solely by a self-interacting Brans--Dicke (BD) scalar field in the absence of ordinary matter. In this framework, the spacetime dynamics are governed solely by the scalar field $Φ$, endowed with a self-interaction potential $V(Φ)$ and non-minimally coupled to the Ricci scalar through the Brans--Dicke action. We numerically solve for the evolution of $Φ(t)$ and the corresponding potential $V(Φ)$ in order to track the collapse dynamics leading to singularity formation. Our analysis demonstrates that, for the energy densities $ρ\approx 1/a$ and $ρ\approx -\ln a$, the collapse inevitably leads to the formation of a central curvature singularity while consistently satisfying the weak energy condition. We further examine the causal structure of the resulting singularity and find that future-directed null geodesics originating from the singularity can propagate to future null infinity, making the singularity globally visible. The strength of the singularity is also examined by extending Tipler's strong curvature condition to the Brans--Dicke field equations. Overall, our findings indicate that gravitational collapse in scalar--tensor gravity can give rise to scenarios that challenge the Cosmic Censorship Conjecture, while underscoring the potential observational relevance of singularities formed through BD scalar-field-driven collapse.

</details>


### [58] [Merger Dynamics of N+N Co-planar Particles in Newton Gravitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07500)
*Qi Su,Baicheng Zhang,Ding-Fang Zeng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过牛顿力学结合广义相对论修正项模拟共面环状天体的并合过程，揭示其动力学与双黑洞系统相似，并生成具有香蕉形畸变和台风状螺旋结构的并合产物；利用精确单体方法计算完整引力波形，定性复现数值相对论结果，为引力波特征与黑洞内部结构间建立直观物理联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在牛顿力学框架中引入广义相对论启发的修正项，模拟两个共面环的并合；采用eXact One-Body方法计算完整引力波形。

Result: 模拟显示‘黑洞’呈现香蕉形变形，并合产物呈台风状螺旋结构；计算得到的引力波形定性上与数值相对论结果一致。

Conclusion: 该环模型能有效类比双黑洞并合动力学，为理解引力波起源及黑洞内部结构提供新视角和补充性物理解释。

Abstract: We model the inspiral and merger dynamics of two co-planar rings in Newtonian mechanics with GR motivated corrections and illustrate their similarity with those of black hole binary systems on the orbital plane. Our simulation reveals a banana-shape deformation of the ``black holes'' involved, and a typhoon-like spiral structure in the merger product. Using an eXact One-Body approach, we compute the full gravitational waveform of this process and qualitatively reproduce results consistent with those of numerical relativity. Our simulation offers a transparent link between the feature of gravitational waveforms and the internal structure of black holes, thus a complementary interpretation of physics behind numerical relativity.

### [59] [Rotation-dependent $I$-Love-$Q$-$δM$ relations in perturbation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07734)
*Eneko Aranguren*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种不依赖于不可观测的静态质量、而基于实际可观测质量的I-Love-Q关系新表述，拓展了其在天体物理观测中的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: I-Love-Q关系虽具理论价值，但其传统归一化形式依赖于不可直接观测的TOV方程导出的静态质量，限制了实际应用。

Method: 采用微扰理论，推导出一组新的归一化量，其定义基于实际（可观测）质量而非静态质量。

Result: 成功构建了不依赖静态质量的I-Love-Q关系新形式，使该关系可直接与观测数据对接。

Conclusion: I-Love-Q关系可被重新参数化以适配可观测质量，从而显著提升其在引力波天文学和中子星物态研究中的实用性。

Abstract: The so-called $I$-Love-$Q$ relations link some normalized versions of the moment of inertia, the Love number, and the quadrupole moment of a star. These relations, in principle, enable the inference of two of the quantities given the third. However, their use has been limited because the normalized versions of the multipole moments rely on the static mass derived from the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equation, which is not directly observable. In this work, using perturbation theory, we find that the $I$-Love-$Q$ relations can also be formulated in terms of an alternative set of normalized quantities that do not depend on the static mass, but on the actual (observable) mass.

### [60] [Epicyclic motion of charged particles around a weakly magnetized Kiselev black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07736)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate the motion of charged particles evolving around a magnetized Kiselev black hole, in the weak magnetic field approximation. The effective potential allows us to study the bound motion and the stable circular orbits. We analyze the impact of combined quintessence and magnetic fields on the epicyclic frequencies. Finally, we examine the periapsis shift and gravitational Larmor precession pointing out differences from the Ernst or Kiselev spacetimes.

### [61] [Exoplanet characterization with NASA's Habitable Worlds Observatory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06233)
*Joanna K. Barstow,Beth Biller,Mei Ting Mak,Sarah Rugheimer,Amaury Triaud,Hannah R. Wakeford*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文讨论了未来NASA的宜居世界天文台（HWO）任务在表征类地行星大气、探测生物标志物和宜居性指标方面的科学目标与技术挑战，并强调英国需加强实验室天体物理与计算建模研究以充分利用该任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前系外行星大气表征虽取得进展，但真正类似太阳系的温带岩质行星和冷气态巨行星仍难以观测；亟需发展高对比度直接成像能力以探测其大气中的分子特征、宜居性乃至生命迹象。

Method: 依托NASA计划于2040年代中期发射的Habitable Worlds Observatory（HWO），利用其冠状仪实现10^{-10}高对比度成像，并结合紫外至近红外波段光谱观测，辅以实验室天体物理实验和先进计算建模支持。

Result: HWO将具备探测海洋反光（ocean glint）、植被‘红边’及关键生物标志气体（如O2、CH4、H2O等）的能力；英国若早期参与（如提供仪器）并持续投入相关基础研究，有望主导后续观测科学产出。

Conclusion: 为确保英国在HWO时代的国际竞争力，必须在未来二十年内对实验室天体物理与计算建模领域提供稳定、持续的资金支持，并积极参与HWO的设计与科学规划。

Abstract: Exoplanet atmosphere characterization has seen revolutionary advances over the last few years, providing us with unique insights into atmospheric chemistry, dynamics and planet formation mechanisms. However, true solar system analog planets remain inaccessible. A major goal for exoplanet science over the coming decades is to observe, and characterize, temperate rocky planets and cool gas giants in orbit around solar-type stars, with the prospect of detecting signs of habitability or even life. Characterization and categorization of these planets relies on direct spectroscopic observations capable of identifying molecular species in their atmospheres; however, these observations represent a substantial engineering challenge due to the extreme contrast between a temperate, Earth-sized exoplanet and its parent star. NASA's next flagship mission, the Habitable Worlds Observatory (HWO) - planned for launch in the mid-2040s - will boast a coronagraphic instrument capable of reaching the needed 10$^{-10}$ contrast, on an ultrastable platform enabling long integration times to achieve the required signal to noise. HWO will cover near-ultraviolet to the near-infrared wavelengths, enabling detections of key biosignature molecules and habitability indicators such as ocean glint and a vegetation `red edge'. Via early involvement in this groundbreaking observatory, including a potential UK instrument contribution, the UK exoplanet community now has an important opportunity to influence the telescope's design. To maintain our international competitiveness, we must be at the forefront of observational campaigns with HWO when it eventually launches, and this comes with the need for parallel development in laboratory astrophysics and computational modelling. Maximising our exploitation of this transformative NASA mission requires consistent financial support in these areas across the next two decades.

</details>


### [62] [Transiting exoplanets as the immediate future for population-level atmospheric science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06236)
*Joanna K. Barstow,Hannah R. Wakeford,Sarah L. Casewell,Vatsal Panwar*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文综述了利用凌星法和掩星法对系外行星大气进行观测与表征的研究进展，强调其在开展系外行星大气群体性研究中的关键作用，并探讨英国在此领域的发展战略与科学领导力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着已发现的凌星系外行星超过6000颗，亟需开展基于大样本的群体级大气研究，以推动大气物理（化学、动力学、云过程、演化）的理解，并关联行星形成机制与宜居性科学目标（如STFC挑战B）。

Method: 主要依赖凌星光谱、掩星光谱及相位曲线观测技术，结合高精度测光与光谱分析，提取行星大气成分、结构与动力学信息。

Result: 确立了当前系外行星大气研究作为唯一可行的大样本研究途径；明确了温度、重力、质量及宿主恒星类型等参数对大气性质的影响路径；为英国参与国际前沿研究提供了战略定位与技术发展建议。

Conclusion: 系外行星大气的群体研究正处于关键转折点，英国应依托现有优势，在观测能力、数据分析与理论建模等方面加强布局，发挥领导作用，服务于基础科学与生命存在条件探索的国家及国际科学目标。

Abstract: The transit method, during which a planet's presence is inferred by measuring the reduction in flux as it passes in front of its parent star, is a highly successful exoplanet detection and characterization technique. During transit, the small fraction of starlight that passes through a planet's atmosphere emerges with the fingerprints of atmospheric gases, aerosols and structure. During eclipse, the relatively small contribution of light from the planet itself may be observed as the planet is occulted by the star. For planets in near-edge-on, short-period orbits, observing the system throughout an entire orbit allows the varying flux from the planet to be extracted as the illuminated `dayside' rotates in and out of view. With spectroscopic observations, we can characterize not only the overall composition of the atmosphere, but also glean insights into atmospheric structure and dynamics. With over 6,000 transiting planets now discovered, such observations are currently our only window into a consistent sample of planetary atmospheres large enough to attempt a population-level study, a critical next step for our understanding of atmospheric science. The vast exoplanet population provides a laboratory for atmospheric physics, including chemistry, dynamics, cloud processes and evolution; extending these results to a larger number of targets will allow us to explore the effects of equilibrium temperature, gravity, mass and parent star type on atmospheric properties, as well as map observable trends to formation scenarios. These findings are critical for addressing STFC's Science Vision Challenge B: how do stars and planetary systems develop and how do they support the existence of life?. Here we outline how the UK must fit within this strategic context, suggest approaches and development for the future, and outline the unique capabilities and leadership of scientists across the UK.

</details>


### [63] [Incorporating Wavefront Error, Wavefront Sensing and Control, and Sensitivities into Exposure Time Calculations for Future Space Missions with the Error Budget Software (EBS)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06342)
*Sarah Steiger,Pin Chen,Laurent Pueyo*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文介绍了为NASA的宜居世界天文台（HWO）任务开发的开源工具Error Budget Software（EBS），用于将波前误差（WFE）、灵敏度和波前传感与控制（WFS&C）等关键参数整合进曝光时间计算，从而提升类地系外行星成像的产量估算精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HWO任务需对约100个恒星系统的宜居带进行光谱观测，并探测约25颗类地行星，这对日冕仪性能（如高透过率、深对比度、宽带性能）及系统稳定性（如波前误差、望远镜不稳定）提出极高要求；而现有曝光时间计算器（ETC）缺乏便捷整合这些关键误差参数的能力。

Method: 开发了开源工具Error Budget Software（EBS），将灵敏度、波前误差（WFE）和波前传感与控制（WFS&C）在多种时空尺度上的影响建模，并直接与开源产量模拟代码EXOSIMS接口，实现端到端曝光时间计算；以USORT望远镜设计方案为例，开展单变量与多变量参数探索分析。

Result: EBS成功实现了对HWO任务中关键误差源（如WFE、探测器噪声、能量分辨率）对曝光时间影响的量化建模，并揭示了原始对比度与波前误差、探测器噪声与能量分辨率之间的趋势关系。

Conclusion: EBS为HWO等未来大型空间日冕仪任务提供了可扩展、可复用的误差预算与曝光时间联合分析框架，显著提升了任务架构评估与仪器设计优化的效率和可靠性。

Abstract: A primary goal of NASA's Habitable Worlds Observatory (HWO) mission concept is to explore the Habitable Zones (HZ) of ~100 stellar systems and acquire spectra of ~25 terrestrial-type planets (with planet/star flux ratios on the order of 1E-10) which places tight constraints on the performance of observatory systems. In particular, coronagraph instrumentation needs to be matured for higher throughput, deeper contrasts, and better broadband performance, while also considering their sensitivity and ability to mitigate the impact of telescope instability and wavefront error (WFE), which can have a profound impact on exo-Earth imaging. The success of various proposed HWO mission architectures is often represented by the estimated exo-Earth candidate yield. Computation of the minimum exposure time to achieve the required signal-to-noise on a given target, using an exposure time calculator (ETC), is a key part of yield estimation. The impacts of coronagraph sensitivity, WFE, and wavefront sensing and control (WFS&C) have been well studied in the context of developing error budgets for missions and instruments such as the Roman Coronagraph Instrument, but there is currently no easily accessible way to incorporate the effects of these key parameters into calculating exposure times for HWO. To address this, we developed the Error Budget Software (EBS) - an open-source tool that synthesizes sensitivity, WFE, and WFS&C information for a variety of temporal and spatial scales and directly interfaces with the open-source yield code EXOSIMS to produce exposure times. We demonstrate how EBS can be used for mission error budgeting using the example of the Ultrastable Observatory Roadmap Team (USORT) observatory design. This includes both single and multi-variate parameter explorations using EBS where we identify trends between raw contrast and wavefront error, and detector noise and energy resolution.

</details>


### [64] [NASA Decadal Astrobiology Research and Exploration Strategy (NASA-DARES 2025) White Paper -- Habitable Worlds Observatory Living Worlds Science Cases: Research Gaps and Needs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06386)
*Niki Parenteau,Giada Arney,Eleanora Alei,Ruslan Belikov,Svetlana,Berdyugina,Dawn Cardace,Ligia F. TL;DR: 本文介绍了宜居世界天文台（HWO）作为首个以天体生物学为目标的天体物理旗舰任务，重点探讨其在邻近恒星周围类地系外行星上搜寻生命迹象的能力，包括定义紫外-可见-近红外波段的生物标志物测量需求、识别解释生物标志物所需的行星及系统信息，以及明确目标恒星的关键属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HWO是首个以搜寻系外岩石行星生命迹象为核心科学目标的天体物理旗舰任务，需系统评估其探测与解释生物标志物的能力，并建立假阳性和假阴性分析框架。

Method: 通过‘活的世界’工作组开展系统性研究，聚焦三方面：（1）识别UV-Vis-NIR波段内具光谱特征的生物标志物并定义其观测要求；（2）确定解释生物标志物所需行星与系统级辅助信息；（3）梳理邻近目标恒星清单并识别其关键先验参数。同时发展了10个补充性天体生物学科学案例。

Result: 确立了大气生物标志物科学案例为HWO望远镜设计的关键驱动力之一；识别出多项关键科研缺口；提出需跨科学任务部协调投入，纳入新制定的跨部门天体生物学战略。

Conclusion: HWO的成功依赖于对生物标志物光谱特性、行星系统背景信息及宿主恒星性质的综合理解；相关研究缺口的填补将决定其在探索‘活的世界’方面的科学回报能力。

Abstract: Executive Summary: The Habitable Worlds Observatory (HWO) is the first astrophysics flagship mission with a key cross-divisional astrobiology science goal of searching for signs of life on rocky planets beyond our solar system. The Living Worlds Working Group under the Science, Technology, and Architecture Review Team (START) was charged with investigating how HWO could characterize potentially habitable exoplanets orbiting stars in the solar neighborhood, search for signs of life, and interpret potential biosignatures within a false positive and false negative framework. In particular, we focused on (1) identifying biosignatures that have spectral features in the UV-Vis-NIR wavelength range and defining their measurement requirements, (2) determining additional information needed from the planet and planet system to interpret biosignatures and assess the likelihood of false positives, and (3) assembling current knowledge of likely HWO target stars and identify which properties of host stars and systems are most critical to know in advance of HWO. The Living Worlds atmospheric biosignatures science case is considered one of the key drivers in the design of the observatory. An additional 10 astrobiology science cases were developed that collectively revealed key research gaps and needs required to fully explore the observatory parameter space and perform science return analyses. Investment in these research gaps will require coordination across the Science Mission Directorate and fall under the purview of the new Division-spanning astrobiology strategy.

</details>

While the core algorithms for predicting and modeling satellite motion have been known for decades, there is a lack of modern, open-source software that implements these algorithms in a way that is accessible to researchers and engineers. brahe is designed to address these challenges by providing a modern, open-source astrodynamics library that is quick-to-deploy, composable, extensible, and easy-to-learn.

### [66] [Computing Natural Magnitudes in the Photometric Systems of Astronomical Plates using Gaia DR3 SEDs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06859)

Main category: astro-ph.IM

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决历史照相底片与现代测光星表之间因光谱响应不匹配导致的光度定标难题，提升历史数据与现代观测的一致性。

Method: 利用Gaia DR3 XP光谱（330–1050 nm）和GaiaXPy库，结合底片乳剂/滤光片实测光谱响应曲线及大气红化修正，通过合成测光计算底片的自然星等和流量；并与APPLAUSE档案中采用传统色项法得到的结果对比。

Result: 在APPLAUSE档案中识别出±0.3 mag及以上的系统误差；新方法能区分相同色指数但不同光度级的恒星，并在高空气质量（~2.0）下实现约0.2 mag的大气红化校正。

Conclusion: 基于Gaia光谱的合成测光法为照相底片提供了更物理、更鲁棒的自然光度系统，显著提升了历史数据的科学可用性与精度。

Abstract: Context. Accurate photometric calibration of astronomical photographic plates remains a fundamental challenge in astronomy, especially when bridging historical photographic data with modern observations due to the mismatch of spectral sensitivities of photographic plates and passbands of modern calibration catalogs. Aims. We intend to derive consistent natural magnitudes for celestial sources within the intrinsic photometric systems of astronomical photographic plates by using Gaia Data Release 3 (DR3) blue photometer (BP) and red photometer (RP) low-resolution spectral data and to show its superiority to former methods. Methods. We compiled spectral characteristic data for emulsions and filters applied in photometric observations using glass plates. The collected color sensitivities, modified by atmospheric reddening depending on the air mass, are then used to compute accurate natural magnitudes and fluxes of objects in the photographic plates through synthetic photometry, utilizing a catalog of Gaia spectral energy distributions (SEDs) over the wavelength range 330 nm to 1050 nm (XP spectra). This process uses GaiaXPy, a Python library designed to handle Gaia DR3 spectral data. These natural magnitudes are then compared with results from the color term method used to compile the data in existing photoplate archives. Results. Comparing the synthetic magnitudes with those existing in the Archives of Photographic PLates for Astronomical USE (APPLAUSE), we were able to reveal systematic errors of the existing data in the range of +/-0.3 mag and higher. In addition, the presented method allows for an accommodation of stars with similar color index but of different luminosity classes as well as an effective correction of atmospheric reddening at higher air masses, approximately 0.2 mag.

### [67] [The Potential Impact of Neuromorphic Computing on Radio Telescope Observatories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07130)
*Nicholas J. Pritchard,Richard Dodson,Andreas Wicenec*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对多种神经形态计算方案在现有及近期射电天文仪器关键处理阶段（尤其是RFI检测）的应用进行系统性分析，涵盖FPGA原型部署与商用神经形态ASIC的功耗与性能评估。

Result: 商用神经形态解决方案可在关键处理环节降低功耗达三个数量级；FPGA上部署SNN可零资本成本为现有设备增添先进数据驱动RFI检测能力；射电望远镜被定位为全球规模最大的‘传感器内计算’挑战，高数据率谱处理是神经形态计算产业的理想应用场景。

Conclusion: 神经形态计算，特别是SNN，为射电天文学提供了现实可行、功耗大幅优化的数据处理新路径，有望从根本上改变天文台的运行预算与技术演进路线。

Abstract: Radio astronomy relies on bespoke, experimental and innovative computing solutions. This will continue as next-generation telescopes such as the Square Kilometre Array (SKA) and next-generation Very Large Array (ngVLA) take shape. Under increasingly demanding power consumption, and increasingly challenging radio environments, science goals may become intractable with conventional von Neumann computing due to related power requirements. Neuromorphic computing offers a compelling alternative, and combined with a desire for data-driven methods, Spiking Neural Networks (SNNs) are a promising real-time power-efficient alternative. Radio Frequency Interference (RFI) detection is an attractive use-case for SNNs where recent exploration holds promise. This work presents a comprehensive analysis of the potential impact of deploying varying neuromorphic approaches across key stages in radio astronomy processing pipelines for several existing and near-term instruments. Our analysis paves a realistic path from near-term FPGA deployment of SNNs in existing instruments, allowing the addition of advanced data-driven RFI detection for no capital cost, to neuromorphic ASICs for future instruments, finding that commercially available solutions could reduce the power budget for key processing elements by up to three orders of magnitude, transforming the operational budget of the observatory. High-data-rate spectrographic processing could be a well-suited target for the neuromorphic computing industry, as we cast radio telescopes as the world's largest in-sensor compute challenge.

### [68] [A free-fall-based switching criterion for P^3 T N-body methods in collisional stellar systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07425)
*Long Wang,David M. Hernandez,Zepeng Zheng,Wanhao Huang*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于自由落体时间的P^3T方法切换准则，用于N体模拟中长程与短程引力作用的划分，并通过petar代码对比了其与传统速度弥散准则在不同星团条件下的能量守恒和双星演化表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: P^3T方法需在保持粒子-树算法效率与粒子-粒子算法精度之间取得平衡，而现有速度弥散（σ）切换准则在低σ或非平衡系统中表现不佳，亟需更鲁棒的切换标准。

Method: 提出基于自由落体时间的PT-PP切换准则，结合petar代码中的P^3T方案与慢速算法正则化技术，对多种初始条件（如维里平衡、亚维里、分形）下的星团进行大量数值模拟，并对比两种准则在能量守恒和双星演化上的差异。

Result: 在维里平衡系统中，自由落体准则对低σ或含双星的松散星团更准确；σ准则更适合高σ系统；在亚维里或分形初态下，自由落体准则随树步长减小而改善，而σ准则因低估二体碰撞而恶化。

Conclusion: 自由落体时间准则是一种更普适、物理意义更明确的PT-PP切换标准，尤其适用于含双星及非平衡态星团的高精度N体模拟。

Abstract: The P$^3$T scheme is a hybrid method for simulating gravitational $N$-body systems. It combines a fast particle-tree (PT) algorithm for long-range forces with a high-accuracy particle-particle (PP, direct $N$-body) solver for short-range interactions. Preserving both PT efficiency and PP accuracy requires a robust PT-PP switching criterion. We introduce a simple free-fall-based switching criterion for general stellar systems, alongside the commonly used velocity-dispersion-based ($σ$-based) criterion. Using the \textsc{petar} code with the P$^3$T scheme and slow-down algorithmic regularization for binaries and higher-order multiples, we perform extensive simulations of star clusters to evaluate how each criterion affects energy conservation and binary evolution. For systems in virial equilibrium, we find that the free-fall-based criterion is generally more accurate for low-$σ$ or loose clusters containing binaries, whereas the $σ$-based criterion is better suited for high-$σ$ systems. Under subvirial or fractal initial conditions, both criteria struggle to maintain high energy conservation; however, the free-fall-based criterion improves as the tree timestep is reduced, whereas the $σ$-based degrades due to its low-accuracy treatment of two-body encounters.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Analysis of 1,938 observational data points to determine mean apparent magnitude and compare brightness against IAU-recommended thresholds.

Result: Mean apparent magnitude is 6.28; 92% of satellites exceed IAU's brightness limit for research interference; 25% impair aesthetic appreciation; reflectivity resembles Starlink v1.

For spacecraft in their operational mode, 92% exceeded the brightness limit recommended by the IAU for interference with research, while 25% distract from aesthetic appreciation of the night sky. The reflective characteristics are similar to Version 1 Starlink spacecraft.

### [71] [Phase structure of heavy dense lattice QCD and three-state Potts model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06446)
*Shinji Ejiri,Masanari Koiida*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文研究了QCD在高温高密下的相变性质，通过构建一个以Polyakov环为动力学变量、受Z₃对称性支配的有效理论，并将其映射为含复外场的三维三态Potts模型，发现随着化学势μ增加，相变由低温区的一级相变经临界点转为交叉，再于高密区恢复一级相变，从而支持QCD重夸克高密区存在一级相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: QCD有限温度相变的性质依赖于粒子密度和动力学夸克质量，尤其在高密度区域尚不明确，需借助有效理论探究其相结构与对称性破缺机制。

Method: 构建高密度重夸克极限下的QCD有效理论，将Polyakov环作为Z₃序参量，引入仅依赖夸克质量m_q和化学势μ的参数C(μ,m_q)控制夸克玻尔兹曼因子；再将Polyakov环替换为Z₃自旋，导出等价的三维三态Potts模型（含复外场），并分析其相图。

Result: 随着化学势μ从0增至∞，相变行为呈现：低密度区为一级相变→临界点处变为交叉→高密度区再次出现一级相变；该结果强烈暗示QCD在高密度重夸克区域存在一级相变。

Conclusion: 基于Z₃对称性与Potts模型映射，本文为QCD高密相结构提供了理论证据，确认重夸克极限下存在一级相变区域，对理解致密星体内部物态及QCD相图具有重要意义。

Abstract: The nature of the finite temperature phase transition of QCD depends on the particle density and the mass of the dynamical quarks. We discuss the properties of the phase transition at high-density, considering an effective theory describing the high-density heavy-quark limit of QCD. This effective theory is a simple model in which the Polyakov loop is a dynamical variable, and the quark Boltzmann factor is controlled by only one parameter, $C(μ,m_q)$, which is a function of the quark mass $m_q$ and the chemical potential $μ$. The Polyakov loop is an order parameter of $Z_3$ symmetry, and the fundamental properties of the phase transition are thought to be determined by the $Z_3$ symmetry broken by the phase transition. By replacing the Polyakov loop with $Z_3$ spin, we find that the effective model becomes a three-dimensional three-state Potts model ($Z_3$ spin model) with a complex external field term. We investigate the phase structure of the Potts model and discuss QCD in the heavy-quark region. As the density varies from $μ=0$ to $μ=\infty$, we find that the phase transition is first order in the low-density region, changes to a crossover at the critical point, and then becomes first order again. This strongly suggests the existence of a first order phase transition in the high-density heavy quark region of QCD.

</details>


### [72] [Lattice QCD determination of the $γZ$ box contribution to the proton weak charge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06582)
*Zhao-long Zhang,Xu Feng,Mikhail Gorchtein,Lu-Chang Jin,Chuan Liu,Chien-Yeah Seng*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文首次通过格点QCD计算了γZ盒图对宇称破坏电子-质子散射的贡献（□γZ），显著降低了该关键理论输入的不确定性，尤其在零能量处将误差缩小一半，并为Mainz P2实验提供了第一性原理支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确测定质子弱荷Q_W^p是检验标准模型的关键，而γZ盒图贡献□γZ是其中主要的理论不确定性来源之一，亟需从第一性原理出发进行高精度计算。

Method: 采用格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）方法，计算电子束能量至155 MeV范围内的γZ盒图贡献，包含轴矢量与矢量分量，并完成连续极限外推。

Result: 在E=0处得到□γZ = 0.00412(9)，误差比先前最精确结果减小两倍；由此导出更新的质子弱荷Q_W^p = 0.06987(50)；同时给出了□γZ的能量依赖关系，为P2实验提供关键理论输入。

Conclusion: 本工作首次实现了γZ盒图贡献的第一性原理格点QCD计算，大幅提升了低能弱相互作用检验的理论精度，增强了未来P2实验提取标准模型参数的可靠性。

Abstract: We present the first lattice QCD determination of the $γZ$ box contribution to parity-violating electron-proton scattering, $\square_{γZ}$ , a key ingredient for the precise tests of the Standard Model via the proton weak charge. Our calculation covers the electron beam energies up to $E =155 MeV$. For the axial-vector component, we achieve reduced uncertainties across the entire energy range compared with phenomenological estimates. For the vector component, the uncertainties remain slightly larger after continuum extrapolation. At $E = 0$, where the vector part vanishes, we obtain $\square_{γZ}= 0.00412(9)$ , reducing the uncertainty by a factor of $2$ relative to the most precise previous determination. Incorporating this result yields an updated weak charge of $Q_{W}^{p}= 0.06987(50)$ . The calculated energy dependence of $\square_{γZ}$ further provides a first-principles input for the upcoming P2 experiment at Mainz, which will operate at the optimized beam energy of $155 MeV$ to extract $Q_{W}^p$.

### [74] [Pion scattering at finite volume within the Inverse Amplitude Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.23462)
*A. Gómez Nicola,R. Molina,Julián A. Sánchez*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文在有限体积下，利用手性微扰理论（ChPT）和逆振幅方法（IAM）研究了π-π散射，并考虑了s、t、u通道及圈图的离散化效应，改进了Veltman-Pasarino恒等式并投影到八面体群不可约表示空间，所得结果对小体积（m_πL ≲ 2）有显著修正，与格点数据一致，有助于提高能量本征值和相移的提取精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 改进有限体积下π-π散射的理论处理，特别是准确刻画多通道离散化效应与左/右割线贡献，以提升格点QCD中能量谱与散射相移提取的精度。

Method: 基于手性微扰理论（ChPT）进行全阶有限体积计算，涵盖s、t、u通道及tadpole圈图的离散化；扩展Veltman-Pasarino恒等式；将振幅投影至八面体群不可约表示空间（使用立方谐波或群表示矩阵）；在此内部空间中构建逆振幅方法（IAM）以获得两π体系能量本征值的完整体积依赖关系。

Result: 在m_πL ≲ 2的小体积区域，相比以往工作存在显著修正；所得能量本征值与现有格点QCD数据兼容；为高精度提取散射相移和低能常数提供了更可靠的理论框架。

Conclusion: 本文提出的有限体积ChPT+IAM方法更全面地包含了多通道离散效应与左/右割线贡献，显著提升了小体积下的理论精度，有望优化格点QCD中强子散射参数的提取流程。

Abstract: We study the effect of a finite volume for pion-pion scattering within Chiral Perturbation Theory (ChPT) and the Inverse Amplitude Method (IAM) in a $L^3$ box (rest frame). Our full ChPT calculation takes into account the discretization not only in the $s$-channel loops but also in the $t,u$- channels and tadpole contributions. Hence, not only the unitarity right-hand cut but also the left-hand one continuum contributions are calculated in the finite volume. A proper extension of the standard Veltman-Pasarino identities is needed, as well as a suitable projection on the internal space spanned by the irreducible representations (irreps) of the octahedral group, based on either a finite set of cubic harmonics or the matrices which represent the irreps properly. From the ChPT we construct the IAM in the internal space, which provides the full volume dependence of the interacting energy levels of two-pions scattering in the finite volume. Our results for various low-energy constants sets show sizable corrections with respect to previous analyses in the literature for $ m_πL \lesssim 2$, being compatible with energy levels lattice data. We expect that our analysis and results will help to optimize the process of determination of energy levels and phase-shifts with higher accuracy.

</details>

### [75] [$T\bar T$ Deformations through BRST Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06247)
*Elia de Sabbata,Pietro Antonio Grassi,Massimo Porrati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过将TT̄变形视为共形场论（CFT）耦合二维动力学引力，利用BRST形式和intertwiner构造，构建了未变形CFT算符到变形理论BRST上同调空间的幺正‘dress’映射；识别出对应CFT原初算符的‘dressed’算符为物理可观测量，并给出基于BRST不变期望值的非微扰关联函数定义，成功复现已知结构与微扰结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为非微扰地理解TT̄变形及其物理可观测量，需超越传统拉格朗日或微扰方法，建立与量子引力耦合的严格框架。

Method: 采用BRST形式主义，结合arXiv:2411.08865提出的intertwiner构造，构建幺正dressing映射；将dressed算符诠释为场依赖的坐标变换，并以此定义非微扰关联函数为BRST不变的期望值。

Result: 获得了未变形CFT算符到TT̄变形后物理可观测量的幺正映射；确认dressed原初算符即为物理可观测量；给出了非微扰定义的关联函数；并验证其与已知结构性质（如形变下的应力张量流方程）及微扰展开一致。

Conclusion: TT̄变形可严格理解为CFT与二维动力学引力的耦合系统，其物理内容由BRST上同调中的dressed算符完全刻画；该构造提供了统一、非微扰且与量子引力图像相容的框架。

Abstract: We study the $T\bar T$ deformation using its formulation as a CFT coupled to two-dimensional dynamical gravity. Working within the BRST formalism, we apply the intertwiner construction of arXiv:2411.08865 to obtain a unitary "dressing" map between undeformed CFT operators and elements of the BRST cohomology of the deformed theory. We identify the resulting "dressed" operators corresponding to CFT primaries as the physical observables of the deformed theory and show that they arise from a field-dependent change of coordinates, in agreement with what is expected for the $T\bar T$ deformation. We then give a non-perturbative definition of deformed correlation functions as BRST-invariant expectation values of dressed operators in the gauge theory. Finally, we verify that our construction reproduces known structural and perturbative results.

</details>

Result: 得到了YB形变参数依赖的Krylov复杂度增长率；当YB参数趋于零时，结果退化为未形变AdS情形。

The full 10d solution contains the $AdS_n (n=2,3)$ as the subspace, along with the dilaton and the background RR and NS fluxes. The Krylov complexity in the dual operator picture is obtained by computing the proper momentum of the massive particle along its geodesic in the bulk spacetime. We explore the effects of YB deformation on the bulk momentum of the particle, which in turn affects the rate of growth of complexity in the dual QFTs. Our results boil down into the undeformed case in the appropriate limit of the YB parameter.

### [79] [Quantum-Corrected Evaporation and Absorption Cross-Section of Near-Extremal Rotating Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06720)
*Shu Luo,Leopoldo A. Pando Zayas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了低温旋转黑洞的霍金蒸发历史，通过考虑近视界、近AdS2喉区的强量子涨落，建立了量子框架与半经典结果的兼容性，揭示了量子修正对晚期蒸发速率的影响，并发现了新的能量衰减规律和量子截面特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了理解低温旋转黑洞在强量子涨落区域（近视界、近AdS2喉区）的霍金蒸发行为，并调和量子效应与半经典结果之间的关系。

Method: 基于包含Schwarzian项和两个规范模的有效作用量，分析Kerr-Newman和Kerr时空中的标量粒子、光子、引力子及旋量粒子的单/双粒子发射过程，并结合超辐射效应与s波通道的平衡进行计算。

Result: 发现量子修正会减缓黑洞晚期蒸发速率；对于小质量、慢旋转、带电黑洞，标量粒子发射导致能量按E(t)∼t^{-8/21}衰减，不同于球对称情形下的t^{-2/5}及半经典t^{-1}；同时揭示了旋转黑洞量子截面的新特征。

Conclusion: 量子效应显著改变旋转黑洞的蒸发动力学，尤其在晚期阶段，超辐射与s波通道接近平衡导致更缓慢的蒸发；该工作为黑洞量子引力性质提供了新见解。

Abstract: We revisit the Hawking evaporation history of low-temperature rotating black holes by taking into consideration the strong quantum fluctuations known to be present in the near-horizon, near-$\mathrm{AdS_2}$ throat region governed by an effective action that includes Schwarzian and two gauge modes. Imposing compatibility of this quantum framework with the semiclassical results creates a novel link between the particle angular momentum and the black hole electric charge before and after emission, leading to a nontrivial interplay between the superradiance effect and other channels. We evaluate single scalar (neutral and charged) emission of Kerr-Newman and single and di-particle emission of photons, gravitons and spinors in the Kerr spacetime. We uncover that quantum corrections may affect late time evaporation rates, which further slows down the whole evaporation process because of the near-balance between the $s$-wave channel and the superradiance channel. Specifically, we find energy decay of the form $E(t)\sim t^{-8/21}$ for scalar emission of a small, slowly rotating and charged black hole which differs from the analogous spherically symmetric quantum correction of $E(t)\sim t^{-2/5}$ already suppressed with respect to the semiclassical rate of $E(t)\sim t^{-1}$. We also discuss the quantum cross section for rotating black holes and point out various new features.

### [80] [Obstructions to Unitary Hamiltonians in Non-Unitary String-Net Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06821)
*Hanshi Yang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了将Levin-Wen弦网形式应用于非幺正球面融合范畴（特别是非幺正Yang-Lee模型）时所遇到的障碍，发现其F符号无幺正解，并从量子维数为负导致Krein空间结构的角度给出解析解释，最终借助PT对称量子力学诠释该非厄米哈密顿量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Levin-Wen弦网形式要求融合范畴是幺正的才能在物理希尔伯特空间上实现；但实际中存在重要非幺正范畴（如Yang-Lee模型），需理解其构造失败的根本原因。

Method: 通过显式构造并验证若干幺正范畴（Rep(D₃)、TY(ℤ₄)、ℤ₇）的哈密顿量来验证框架；对Yang-Lee模型采用定制的流形梯度下降算法优化F符号；结合代数分析证明负量子维数导致不定度规（Krein空间）；引入PT对称量子力学框架进行物理解释。

Result: Yang-Lee融合规则不存在满足pentagon方程的幺正F符号解；负量子维数必然导致弦网空间具有不定内积，即Krein空间而非希尔伯特空间；相应哈密顿量虽非厄米，但在PT对称意义下仍可具有实谱，且该障碍源于融合环本身，无法通过幺正规范变换消除。

Conclusion: 非幺正融合范畴无法直接用于标准Levin-Wen弦网构造，因其内在代数结构（如负量子维数）导致物理态空间失去正定内积；但可通过PT对称等广义量子框架赋予其物理意义，拓展了拓扑序与非厄米物理的交叉理解。

Abstract: The Levin-Wen string-net formalism provides a canonical mapping from spherical fusion categories to local Hamiltonians defining Topological Quantum Field Theories (TQFTs). While the topological invariance of the ground state is guaranteed by the pentagon identity, the realization of the model on a physical Hilbert space requires the category to be unitary. In this work, we investigate the obstructions arising when this construction is applied to non-unitary spherical categories, specifically the Yang-Lee model (the non-unitary minimal model $\mathcal{M}(2,5)$). We first validate our framework by explicitly constructing and verifying the Hamiltonians for rank-3 ($\text{Rep}(D_3)$), rank-5 ($\text{TY}(\mathbb{Z}_4)$), and Abelian ($\mathbb{Z}_7$) unitary categories. We then apply this machinery to the non-unitary Yang-Lee model. Using a custom gradient-descent optimization algorithm on the manifold of $F$-symbols, we demonstrate that the Yang-Lee fusion rules admit no unitary solution to the pentagon equations. We explain this failure analytically by proving that negative quantum dimensions impose an indefinite metric on the string-net space, realizing a Krein space rather than a Hilbert space. Finally, we invoke the theory of $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric quantum mechanics to interpret the non-Hermitian Hamiltonian, establishing that the obstruction is intrinsic to the fusion ring and cannot be removed by unitary gauge transformations.

</details>


### [81] [$E$ and $J$ type $\mathcal{N}=(0,2)$ disordered models and higher-spin symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06923)
*Liang Wang,Miao Wang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了2维N=(0,2)无序模型中高自旋结构的涌现，扩展了先前仅考虑J型模型的工作，纳入E型势，并通过Landau-Ginzburg理论建立两类模型的对偶性；利用Schwinger-Dyson方程和四点函数的梯形核矩阵分析，证实E型与J型模型在红外下动力学等价，且E型模型在特定极限下也呈现涌现高自旋对称性，拓展了模空间认知，并为有限张力到无张力弦的全息相变提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作局限于忽略Fermi多重态中E项的J型模型，本文旨在将分析推广至更一般的含E型势的N=(0,2)无序模型，探索其是否同样支持高自旋对称性涌现及对应全息含义。

Method: 基于（无序）N=(0,2) Landau-Ginzburg理论构建模型对偶；求解Schwinger-Dyson方程及四点函数的梯形核矩阵，分析红外行为；考察E型模型在特定极限下的对称性结构。

Result: E型模型与J型模型在红外下动力学等价；E型模型在特定极限下亦展现出涌现的高自旋对称性；揭示了更大范围的2D N=(0,2)无序理论模空间，并关联到全息中有限张力向无张力弦的相变。

Conclusion: 含E型势的N=(0,2)无序模型同样支持高自旋对称性涌现，表明该现象比此前认知更具普适性；这一结果深化了对二维超对称无序系统及其全息对偶的理解。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the emergence of higher-spin structure in 2d $\mathcal{N}=(0,2)$ disordered models. While previous studies focused on the $J$-type model where the $E$-term in the Fermi multiplet was discarded. We extend the discussion to $\mathcal{N}=(0,2)$ disordered models with $E$-type potential. In terms of (disordered) $\mathcal{N}=(0,2)$ Landau-Ginzburg theory, we establish a duality between two models. By solving the Schwinger-Dyson equations and the ladder kernel matrix for 4-point functions, we verify that the $E$-type model is dynamically equivalent to the $J$-type model in the IR regime. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the $E$-type model also exhibits emergent higher-spin symmetry in certain limits. Our results reveal a larger region of the moduli space of 2D $\mathcal{N}=(0,2)$ disordered theories and provides insights into the holographic transition from finite to tensionless strings that can be diagnosed by the emergence of higher-spin symmetries.

Result: 得到了OPE系数至ε一阶的显式表达式。

### [83] [Classical Unattainability of Extremality in non-BPS D-brane Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07032)
*Pranav Kumar,Swapnamay Mondal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了N=8弦理论中一个非BPS极端四荷Reissner-Nordstrom黑洞的经典世界线理论，发现其微观D膜描述即使在经典层面也无法实现真正的极端态，存在正的最小能量，这源于D膜导致的超对称破缺模式，并影响近视界AdS2稳定性及黑洞熵的构型解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期引力结果暗示极端性（零基态能量）这一精细调节条件可能无法满足，但尚不清楚这是量子效应还是经典效应；本文旨在探究该问题在经典层面的表现。

Method: 分析N=8弦理论中非BPS极端四荷Reissner-Nordstrom黑洞的世界线理论，研究其微观D-brane描述下的经典态结构与超对称破缺模式。

Result: 发现D-brane系统在经典层面即不存在严格的极端态，存在正的最小能量；该能量源于D-brane引起的超对称破缺；黑洞熵对应于微观势能中孤立极小值的数目之对数，即构型熵；同时还存在对应于D-brane弱束缚态的多个局域极小值连续谱。

Conclusion: 极端性在经典层面即被破坏，正基态能量是超对称破缺的直接结果，它不仅挑战近视界AdS2稳定性，也表明黑洞熵本质上是微观构型熵。

Abstract: For the worldline theory of an extremal black hole, extremality amounts to vanishing ground state energy. In light of recent gravity results one would expect much like the ground state degeneracy this fine tuned condition too will not be met. It is unclear though whether this should be a quantum artefact or classical. In this paper we consider a non-BPS extremal four-charge Reissner Nordstrom black hole in N = 8 String theory. It is shown that the microscopic D-brane description fails to admit any extremal state, even classically. This positive energy is expected to destabilize the near horizon AdS2. The positive minimum energy is a direct consequence of the pattern of supersymmetry breaking by the D-branes. The black hole entropy is found to be the logarithm of the number of isolated minima and hence is related to the configurational entropy of the microscopic potential. We also find multiple continua of local minima corresponding to marginally bound states of the constituent D-branes.

### [84] [Boundary flow and geometric realization in holographic $T\bar T$-deformed BCFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07509)
*Feiyu Deng*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从场论内在视角研究了边界共形场论（BCFT）的 $T\bar{T}$ 变形，提出一种不依赖有限径向截断的渐近变分原理来定义该变形，并导出应力张量的精确二次迹关系；发现当无独立边界自由度时，变形可完全局域化于边界，且在反射边界条件下退化为仅由位移算符驱动的一维无关流；通过闭式积分得到诱导边界作用量，表明变形仅重组原有边界数据；并建立了固定边界与移动边界的等价性；在全息对应中区分了AdS₃/BCFT₂的Type A与Type B两种实现，利用纠缠熵揭示了内禀边界流的普适特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解边界共形场论（BCFT）在$T\bar{T}$变形下的内在场论结构，避免依赖人为截断，厘清边界局部化变形的本质及其全息实现的物理含义。

Method: 基于AdS₃中的渐近变分原理公式化$T\bar{T}$变形，推导应力张量的精确二次迹关系；分析反射边界条件下的位移算符作用；闭式积分求解边界无关流；构造诱导边界作用量；对比Type A与Type B全息实现，并用零温与有限温纠缠熵进行区分。

Result: 获得不依赖径向截断的$T\bar{T}$变形基本定义；证明无独立边界自由度时变形完全边界局域化；发现反射边界下变形退化为仅由位移算符决定的一维无关流；给出闭式诱导边界作用量；建立固定/移动边界的变分等价性；明确Type A与Type B全息实现的物理差异，并通过纠缠熵提取普适边界流效应。

Conclusion: BCFT的$T\bar{T}$变形本质上是一种内在的、边界局域化的无关流，不引入新边界自由度，而是重组原有边界数据；其全息实现（Type A/B）影响表观现象（如边界位移），但普适动力学由位移算符主导；该框架统一了不同边界描述，并为BCFT的可积变形与全息RG流提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the $T\bar T$ deformation of boundary conformal field theories (BCFTs) from an intrinsic field-theoretic perspective. Formulating the deformation as a modification of the asymptotic variational principle in AdS$_3$, we obtain the exact quadratic trace relation for the stress tensor without introducing a finite radial cutoff, which we take as the fundamental definition of the deformed theory. When restricted to a BCFT without independent boundary degrees of freedom, the intrinsic $T\bar T$ deformation becomes genuinely boundary-localized. Imposing reflective boundary conditions collapses the bulk composite operator to a universal one-dimensional irrelevant flow governed entirely by the displacement operator. We integrate this flow in closed form and derive an induced boundary action, showing that the deformation reorganizes existing boundary data without introducing new boundary degrees of freedom. We further establish a precise equivalence between a fixed-boundary description and a moving-boundary description, interpreted as a reparametrization of the variational problem rather than physical boundary dynamics.
  On the holographic side, we analyze two inequivalent realizations in AdS$_3$/BCFT$_2$, referred to as Type~A and Type~B. In Type~A, a rigid cutoff surface intersects the end-of-the-world brane at finite position, leading to an apparent boundary displacement. In Type~B, the cutoff surface is asymptotically AdS$_2$, so that the BCFT boundary is geometrically pinned and the displacement operator vanishes identically. Using entanglement entropy at zero and finite temperature, we disentangle universal consequences of the intrinsic boundary-localized flow from features that depend on the holographic implementation.

</details>

Method: 采用等变局部化；对奇维内部空间沿收缩圆进行维度约化，从而在剩余偶维时空引入边界；在考虑边界贡献后，在该偶维时空上执行标准偶维局部化；将方法应用于多种超对称AdS3解，尤其关注穿孔黎曼面上的紧致化。

Conclusion: 该工作为AdS3/CFT2对应中涉及穿孔和缺陷的模型提供了新的局部化工具，揭示了超对称守恒量与几何穿孔结构之间的深层联系，并拓展了超引力中局部化技术的应用范围。

Abstract: We use equivariant localization to compute various observables for $\mathcal{N}=(2,2)$ preserving AdS$_3$ solutions in type IIB supergravity. Our method for localizing the odd-dimensional internal space is to perform a dimensional reduction along a shrinking circle which introduces a boundary in the remaining even-dimensional spacetime. Canonical even-dimensional localization can then be performed on this space after taking into account contributions from the boundary. We illustrate with a number of supersymmetric solutions. One of the novel aspects of this work is applying these techniques to study punctures and defects using localization. We obtain new results for the central charge of 2d SCFTs arising from compactifying $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM on a punctured Riemann surface.

Abstract: In holographic duality, the total energy of the dual field theory is obtained from the holographic renormalization, which depends not only on the bulk geometry but also on the choice of quantization schemes. We point out that the validity of several widely studied holographic inequalities -- including the AdS Penrose inequality, the late-time bound on entanglement entropy growth, and the growth-rate limits of CV and CA complexities -- depends on the choice of quantization schemes. Motivated by this issue, we introduce a modified total energy, which is still computed via holographic renormalization but the final value is independent of the choice of quantization schemes. We verify that this new ``total energy'' restores all these bounds to universal validity in the model of generalized free scalar field theory. Abstract: We study an Aganagic-Vafa brane supported on a special Lagrangian submanifold $\mathcal{L}$ in a non-compact toric Calabi-Yau threefold $\mathcal{X}$. ### [88] [Spacetime Quasicrystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07769)
*Latham Boyle,Sotirios Mygdalas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper introduces Lorentzian quasicrystals—generalizations of Euclidean self-similar quasicrystals (e.g., Penrose tilings) to Minkowski spacetime—and explores their novel properties and speculative physical implications, including a possible link to the seesaw relation among fundamental energy scales via embedding in a (9+1)D symmetric torus.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To extend the mathematical beauty and structural richness of self-similar quasicrystals from Euclidean space to relativistic spacetime, and to explore potential connections to fundamental physics, especially the hierarchy of energy scales in nature.

Method: Constructing explicit examples of Lorentzian quasicrystals by adapting cut-and-project methods and symmetry principles to Minkowski spacetime; analyzing their discrete scale invariance, quasiperiodicity, and Lorentz covariance; and speculating on physical realizations using string-theoretic compactifications.

Result: First explicit constructions of Lorentzian quasicrystals (spacetime analogues of Penrose/Ammann-Beenker tilings); identification of key distinguishing features (e.g., causal structure compatibility, modified scaling symmetries); and a speculative embedding scenario linking a (3+1)D universe into a (9+1)D symmetric torus that may explain the seesaw relation $M_{\rm Pl}M_{\rm vac}\approx M_{\rm EW}^{2}$.

Conclusion: Lorentzian quasicrystals are mathematically consistent, geometrically rich structures with potentially profound physical relevance—offering a novel geometric framework to address long-standing questions about spacetime structure, symmetry, and fundamental scales.

Abstract: Self-similar quasicrystals (like the famous Penrose and Ammann-Beenker tilings) are exceptional geometric structures in which long-range order, quasiperiodicity, non-crystallographic orientational symmetry, and discrete scale invariance are tightly interwoven in a beautiful way. In this paper, we show how such structures may be generalized from Euclidean space to Minkowski spacetime. We construct the first examples of such Lorentzian quasicrystals (the spacetime analogues of the Penrose or Ammann-Beenker tilings), and point out key novel features of these structures (compared to their Euclidean cousins). We end with some (speculative) ideas about how such spacetime quasicrystals might relate to reality. This includes an intriguing scenario in which our infinite $(3+1)$D universe is embedded (like one of our spacetime quasicrystal examples) in a particularly symmetric $(9+1)$D torus $T^{9,1}$ (which was previously found to yield the most symmetric toroidal compactification of the superstring). We suggest how this picture might help explain the mysterious seesaw relationship $M_{\rm Pl}M_{\rm vac}\approx M_{\rm EW}^{2}$ between the Planck, vacuum energy, and electroweak scales ($M_{\rm Pl}$, $M_{\rm vac}$, $M_{\rm EW}$).

</details>


### [89] [Black holes and causal nonlinear electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07789)
*Jorge G. Russo,Paul K. Townsend*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了非线性电动力学（NLED）理论中球对称带电黑洞解的因果性限制，发现对于一大类非因果Born型NLED理论，Reissner-Nordstrom（RN）度规是某些双荷黑洞的精确但不稳定解；而对于所有因果NLED理论，则不存在正则黑洞，且固定电荷下极端黑洞的熵小于RN熵；此外还分析了RN型与Schwarzschild型全局结构之间的参数空间相变条件，并指出Schwarzschild型向裸奇点转变时，在有限质量处对应的度规为Barriola-Vilenkin整体单极子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨非线性电动力学（NLED）中因果性对球对称带电黑洞解的限制，特别是其对黑洞结构、稳定性及热力学性质的影响。

Method: 基于爱因斯坦-NLED方程，对球对称带电黑洞解进行因果性分析，结合稳定性判据、熵比较与全局结构分类方法，研究不同NLED理论下的解性质。

Result: 1) 对于非因果Born型NLED，RN度规是某些双荷黑洞的精确但不稳定解；2) 所有因果NLED均无正则黑洞，且固定电荷下极端黑洞熵小于RN熵；3) 存在RN型与Schwarzschild型全局结构的参数空间相变；4) Schwarzschild型向裸奇点转变的临界点对应Barriola-Vilenkin整体单极子度规。

Conclusion: 因果性对NLED黑洞解具有强约束：排除正则黑洞，降低极端黑洞熵，并决定全局结构相变行为；非因果理论虽允许RN解，但其不稳定性削弱物理可实现性。

Abstract: For generic theories of nonlinear electrodynamics (NLED) we investigate the restrictions imposed by causality on spherically-symmetric charged black-hole solutions of the Einstein-NLED equations. For a large class of (acausal) Born-type NLED theories, we find that the Reissner-Nordstrom (RN) metric is an exact, but unstable, solution for some dyonic black holes. For all causal NLED we show that there are no regular black holes, and that the entropy of extremal black holes is less than the RN entropy for fixed charge. We also find the conditions for a parameter-space transition between RN-type and Schwarzschild-type global structure. For the transition from Schwarzschild-type to naked singularity, which occurs at finite mass, we show that the metric at the transition point is a Barriola-Vilenkin global monopole.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Drell-Yan与SIDIS的交叉对称性，构建阈值重求和框架；区分双软极限（Bjorken x 和碎裂z 同时趋近1）与单软极限（仅x→1 或仅z→1），分别识别主导辐射模式（软或准直），并结合最近的NNLO固定阶结果拟合重求和系数。

Abstract: We derive threshold resummation of semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering (SIDIS), by building upon previous results by some of us for the resummation of the Drell-Yan process at fixed rapidity, which is related to SIDIS by crossing. We consider both a double-soft limit, in which both the Bjorken and the fragmentation scaling variables tend to their threshold value, and single soft limits in which either of them does. We show that in the former limit only soft radiation contributes, and in the latter limit only collinear radiation, and we derive resummed expressions for the coefficient functions in all cases. We determine explictly resummation coefficients in the nonsinglet channel up to next-to-next-to-leading log by comparing to recent fixed next-to-next-to-leading order results. Expanding out the single-soft resummation we reproduce recent next-to-leading power results.

Abstract: In this work, we study leptonic decays of hadrons as probes of light neutrinophilic scalars that mediate enhanced neutrino self-interactions. Using these results, we derive the projected sensitivity of PIONEER and assess the current and future reach of BeEST. The resulting low-energy spectral tails provide a characteristic signal for light neutrinophilic scalars, making upcoming hadron decay experiments powerful probes of light mediators of non-standard neutrino self-interactions.

### [93] [One-loop renormalization and $\boldsymbolρ$ parameter in the Georgi-Machacek model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06252)
*Debtosh Chowdhury,Anirban Kundu,Poulami Mondal,Subrata Samanta,Aaryan Srivastava*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究Georgi-Machacek模型的一圈重整化，重点分析其对电弱ρ参数的紫外发散修正及其对电弱精度观测量的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Georgi-Machacek模型在树图水平具有全局SU(2)_R对称性，导致某些算符缺失；而一圈修正可打破该对称性，从而引入新的现象学重要效应，特别是对电弱ρ参数的影响。

Method: 通过将所有树图参数用标准输入参数α_e、G_μ和m_Z表示，系统计算一圈修正，并分析模型参数（如五重态与单态质量差、二重态与三重态真空期望值之比、单态CP偶标量混合角）对ρ参数一圈修正的定量影响。

Result: 发现一圈修正下ρ参数呈现紫外发散；需四个输入参数才能完全描述一圈精度下的电弱可观测量；ρ参数对五重态与单态质量差仅呈弱依赖，主要依赖于二重态与三重态真空期望值之比及单态CP偶标量的混合角。

Conclusion: Georgi-Machacek模型的一圈重整化对电弱精度检验至关重要，ρ参数的行为揭示了模型关键参数的物理约束，为未来实验验证提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study the one-loop renormalization of the Georgi-Machacek model. At one loop, the renormalization of the model is phenomenologically important when triggered by operators that are absent at the tree level due to the global $SU(2)_R$ symmetry. By computing all the tree-level parameters from the standard input parameters $α_e$, $G_μ$, and $m_Z$, we show the ultraviolet divergent nature of the electroweak $ρ$ parameter when one-loop corrections are incorporated. In this model, four input parameters are required to completely parametrize the electroweak precision observables at one loop. We study the quantitative impact of the model parameters on the one-loop corrections to the $ρ$ parameter. At one loop, the $ρ$ parameter shows a mild dependence on the mass differences between the custodial fiveplet and the heavy custodial singlet, and mainly depends on the ratio of the doublet and triplet vacuum expectation values, and on the mixing angle between the custodial singlet CP-even scalars.

We find that PIONEER can improve bounds on exotic pion branching ratios by at least one order of magnitude below current limits. We compare the projected sensitivities with complementary constraints from lepton anomalous magnetic moments, mono-photon searches, and beam-dump experiments, identifying weak-violating axion-like particles as a particularly well-motivated benchmark. Using a modified version of the BBN code \faGithub \href{https://github.com/vallima/PRyMordial}{\,\texttt{PRyMordial}} with dynamically-solved chemical potentials and appropriate finite-mass corrections, we constrain electron-positron mass differences from observed abundances of Helium-4, Deuterium, and $N_{\rm eff}$. We present three toy models demonstrating how $b_0(T) \propto T^2$ arises from field-theoretic mechanisms, including temperature-driven phase transitions. These results provide the most stringent constraints on early-universe CPT violation in this regime, probing parameter space inaccessible to laboratory experiments.

In this framework, all left-handed fermions are neutral, while right-handed fermions of the third generation carry charges distinct from those of the first two generations. This structure naturally explains the observed Standard Model fermion mass hierarchy: the heavy masses of the third generation are generated at tree level, while the lighter masses of the first and second generations arise radiatively at the one-loop level. Abstract: We investigate the internal structure of the ground ($1S$) and the first two radially excited ($2S,3S$) states of the pion within the light-front quark model. The valence Fock sector is described using pure harmonic-oscillator eigenstates and mixed states formed as orthogonal linear combinations of these eigenfunctions. The optimal wavefunction parameters are determined through a variational procedure based on a QCD-motivated effective Hamiltonian. Using the resulting light-front wavefunctions, we study the pion distribution amplitude, parton distribution function, and electromagnetic form factor. After QCD evolution, the ground state distribution amplitude and parton distribution function are found to be in good agreement with available experimental data. At the model scale, the parton distribution functions of the $1S$ and $2S$ states show clear sensitivity to state mixing, while the distribution amplitudes and electromagnetic form factors are weakly sensitive. The decay constants of the mixed states are also found to decrease sequentially with increasing radial excitation.

Method: 引入Z3分级结构，构造具有实质量与共轭复质量的三重Lee-Wick型纠缠场；将六个Pauli旋量（含色与反色）统一为12分量广义旋量；定义12×12广义γ矩阵，建立广义Dirac方程；分析其六阶色散关系及渐近行为；构造三次组合以抵消衰减因子。

Abstract: We propose a description of colour triplets of quarks by entangled Z3-graded Lee-Wick type fields, one with real mass and the two remaining ones with mutually conjugate complex masses. The so entangled triplet of quark fields satisfies a generalized Dirac equation, with generalized 12x1é gamma-matrices acting on 12-component coloured spinors. The sixth order dispersion relations lead to solutions suitably vanishing in asymptotic region, exhibiting the well established confinement property of coloured quarks' degrees of freedom. We show how one can construct certain cubic combinations of those solutions in a way that cansels the damping factors, producing freely propagating functions.
