Abstract: We investigate low-energy $Nφ$ scattering driven by a pole-enhanced triangle diagram, in which the two-kaon-exchange contribution is promoted by the near-threshold $Λ(1405)$ pole in the $N\bar K$ subsystem. Using an unphysical kaon mass motivated by lattice simulations, we evaluate the $Nφ$ scattering length and find that this mechanism generates an attractive interaction with a magnitude of $-1.5$ to $-0.5,\rm{fm}$. Spin-dependent effects are not treated explicitly and are expected to provide subleading corrections in the near-threshold region. We further analyze the low-energy behavior of the triangle-diagram amplitude and show that the scattering length performs a characteristic power-law dependence on the parameter $\tildeδ$, defined as the mass difference between the $K\bar K$ threshold and the $φ$ meson. This threshold-driven behavior differs from that associated with van der Waals-type forces or the long-range tail of two-pion exchange, highlighting the role of three-body dynamics encoded in the pole-enhanced triangle diagram in shaping the near-threshold $Nφ$ interaction.

The analysis is carried out with all-flavour neutrino interactions, where we demonstrate that cascade events, primarily due to $ν_{e,τ}$, show greater sensitivity to a dark matter signal compared to the more commonly studied track events. Furthermore, we highlight the impact of a previously overlooked background, Galactic neutrinos produced from interactions between hadronic cosmic rays and interstellar gas. We find dark matter sensitivities are more strongly degraded in the high energy region above $\sim 10\, {\rm TeV}$, with a maximal weakening of approximately a factor of $\sim 2$. This effect remains smaller than the uncertainty associated with the dark matter density profile but can nonetheless mimic a positive annihilation signal. We contextualize these results with a concrete particle model and show that TRIDENT will be able to probe the most interesting untested parts of parameter space.

### [104] [Quarkonium light-cone distribution amplitudes: twist structure and mass dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06825)
*Shuai Xu,Xiao-Nan Li,Jin-Zhong Han,Bai-hui Cheng,Li-li Chen,Qin Chang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了基态赝标量和矢量夸克偶素的领头阶和次领头阶光锥分布振幅（LCDAs），发现其Gegenbauer矩、ξ-矩和横向动量矩具有由夸克质量驱动的普适演化规律，并在重夸克极限下呈现扭度无关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解夸克偶素光锥分布振幅（LCDAs）随夸克质量变化的系统性行为，及其在强子物理与QCD因子化中的关键作用。

Method: 在光前夸克模型（LFQM）框架下，通过替换M→M₀分析赝标量和矢量夸克偶素的纵向与横向LCDAs结构，并计算其Gegenbauer矩、ξ-矩和横向动量矩；利用电荷共轭对称性约束奇数矩为零。

Result: 发现电荷共轭对称性导致所有奇数Gegenbauer矩和ξ-矩严格为零；赝标量偶素的扭度2与3 LCDAs完全相同；矢量偶素在重夸克极限下各扭度LCDAs趋同（φ^A₂ ≈ φ^P₃ ≈ φ^∥₂ ≈ φ^⊥₃）；LCDAs随夸克质量增大而变尖锐、窄化，峰值服从m/β标度律，横向动量矩随质量增大而上升。

Conclusion: 夸克偶素LCDAs展现出由夸克质量主导的普适演化规律：从相对论性向非相对论性束缚态过渡，并在重夸克极限下出现扭度无关性，揭示了QCD中夸克质量对强子内部结构的深刻调控作用。

Abstract: We present a systematic study of the leading- and next-to-leading-twist light-cone distribution amplitudes (LCDAs) of ground-state pseudoscalar and vector quarkonium within the light-front quark model (LFQM). By implementing the replacement $M \to M_0$, we analyze the longitudinal and transverse structures of the LCDAs, together with their Gegenbauer moments, $ξ$-moments, and transverse momentum moments. We show that charge-conjugation symmetry enforces the exact vanishing of all odd Gegenbauer moments and odd $ξ$-moments. For pseudoscalar quarkonium, the twist-2 and twist-3 LCDAs become identical, which lead to their Gegenbauer moments, $ξ$-moments, and transverse momentum moments are the same, respectively. For vector quarkonium, although the twist-2 and twist-3 LCDAs differ in the case of masses quark, they progressively converge as the quark mass increases. In the heavy-quark limit, all quarkonium LCDAs satisfy $φ^A_{2} = φ^P_{3} \simeq φ^{\parallel}_{2} \simeq φ^{\perp}_{3}$, demonstrating an emergent twist-independence of quarkonium distribution amplitudes. We further find that the LCDAs become increasingly peaked and narrower with increasing quark mass, reflecting the meson system becomes increasingly close to a nonrelativistic bound state, with a more uniform and stable distribution of internal longitudinal momentum. For all quarkonium, the peak value exhibits a simple phenomenological scaling behavior governed by the ratio $m/β$. The transverse momentum moments increase with the meson mass, indicating a progressively more compact bound-state structure. These results reveal a universal and systematic evolution of quarkonium LCDAs driven by the quark mass.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 概念性分析，对比θ=0与θ≠0情形下对拓扑、拓扑荷密度定义、粗粒化规范场、瞬子及反常等假设的依赖程度。

Abstract: On the basis of allowed local gauge symmetries, the QCD Lagrangian admits a CP-violating term proportional to the topological charge density, commonly referred to as the $θ$ term. A priori, any value of $θ$ is consistent with the local symmetries of the theory, while current experimental limits constrain $θ\lesssim 10^{-10}$. The apparent extreme smallness of this parameter is known as the strong $CP$ problem.
  In this work, we provide a careful critical overview of the conceptual assumptions underlying the $θ$ term, focusing on the roles of topology, the definition of topological charge density, rough gauge field configurations, instantons, and anomalies. We contrast the assumptions required to describe QCD at nonzero $θ$ with those sufficient at $θ= 0$, and argue that a vanishing $θ$ term is compatible with a formulation based solely on local gauge invariance and causal locality, without invoking additional global structure.
  The perspective developed here is intended as a conceptual analysis of the standard formulation of the strong $CP$ problem. It does not challenge the internal consistency of QCD at nonzero $θ$, nor does it diminish the independent theoretical and phenomenological motivation for axion and axion-like particle physics, which are well-motivated extensions of the Standard Model.

### [109] [Exclusive Decays of the Fully Heavy Tetraquarks into Light Mesons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07243)

Result: 估算得 $T_{4c} \to π^+π^-$ 衰变宽度约 $10^{-9}$ GeV，$T_{4b} \to π^+π^-$ 约 $10^{-14}$ GeV；对应分支比约 $10^{-8}$，当前实验不可观测；揭示了多粒子过程特有的 $i\varepsilon$ 规范必要性。

Conclusion: 该衰变过程虽目前不可观测，但其理论结构揭示了多粒子硬排它过程的新特征；所发展的扇区分解方法具有一般适用性，可推广至如 $T_{4c,b} \to p\bar{p}$ 等类似过程。

We estimate the decay widths to be $10^{-9}$ GeV and $10^{-14}$ GeV for the decays $T_{4c} \to π^+π^-$ and $T_{4b} \to π^+π^-$ (and similarly for $K^+K^-$), respectively. The branching ratio for $T_{4c} \to π^+π^-(K^+K^-)$ is on the order of $10^{-8}$, making it currently unobservable in existing experiments. The factorization of $T_{4c,b}$ into light hadrons shares similarities with the decay $J/ψ\to p\bar{p}$. However, unlike the latter process, the decay $T_{4c,b} \to π^+π^-(K^+K^-)$ exhibits unique features that arise only in processes involving multiple incoming or outgoing particles. One such feature is the necessity of maintaining the $i\varepsilon$-prescription for the denominators or propagators due to the divergences in the kinematic region of interest. Employing the sector decomposition method, along with the aid of the Cheng-Wu theorem and the {\tt QHull} program, we present a systematic approach to handle the convolutions and phase-space integrations. This method can also be extended to similar processes, such as $T_{4c,b} \to p\bar{p}$, as well as to phase-space integrations where each denominator is a linear combination of integration variables.

TL;DR: 本文在深度非弹性散射的偶极子图像中引入有限能量约束，限制虚光子-靶心质心系能量下的产生强子系统的不变质量，并研究其对粲夸克和轻夸克产额的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在深度非弹性散射的偶极子图像中，通常忽略能量守恒对部分子系统产生的限制；本文旨在引入并量化有限能量约束的影响，以更精确描述高能QCD过程。

Method: 通过将虚光子-靶心质心系能量作为产生的部分子系统不变质量上限，修正偶极子模型中的截面计算，并数值评估该约束在不同x和Q²下的影响。

Result: 在Q²=1 GeV²、x=0.01时，该约束使粲夸克贡献减少约35%，轻夸克减少约7%；但随x减小或Q²增大，效应迅速减弱。

Conclusion: 有限能量约束在中等Q²和较大x区域不可忽略，尤其对重夸克产生有显著抑制作用，需在偶极子模型中予以考虑。

Abstract: We implement a finite energy constraint in the dipole picture of deep inelastic scattering by restricting the invariant mass of the produced partonic system by the virtual photon-target center of mass energy. We show that, for $Q^2=1$GeV$^2$, the effect of this constraint can reach up to $\sim$35% for charm quarks and $\sim$7% for light quarks at $x=0.01$, but then rapidly decreases at smaller $x$ or larger $Q^2$.

### [112] [Probing the spin parity structure of hidden charm pentaquarks from spectroscopy and magnetic moments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07323)
*Pallavi Gupta*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在重子-介子分子框架下，利用Gursey-Radicati质量公式研究了隐粲五夸克态的自旋宇称JP分配，并通过全局拟合41个已知强子质量确定参数；结果将Pc(4312)、Pc(4440)、Pc(4457)分别指派为JP=1/2、3/2、5/2，将带奇异数的Pcs(4459)解释为SU(3)八重态中JP=3/2的奇异成员；进一步计算了磁矩，其系统行为满足求和规则，表明磁矩可作为未来鉴别五夸克态量子数的有用观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验上已发现多个隐粲五夸克态，但其自旋宇称（JP）量子数尚未明确；需建立理论框架以合理分配JP并寻找可验证的可观测量来辅助确认。

Method: 采用重子-介子分子模型，结合Gursey-Radicati质量公式构建隐粲五夸克质量谱；通过全局拟合41个已知强子质量确定模型参数；基于质量谱对实验观测态进行JP分配；构造显式波函数计算各态磁矩，并检验SU(3)多重态及不同JP下的磁矩求和规则。

Result: 成功将Pc(4312)、Pc(4440)、Pc(4457)分别指派为JP = 1/2、3/2、5/2；将Pcs(4459)解释为SU(3)八重态中JP = 3/2的奇异成员；计算得到的磁矩满足理论预期的求和规则，展现出系统性规律。

Conclusion: 该分子框架能自洽地解释现有隐粲五夸克态的质量与JP分配；磁矩作为敏感观测量，有望在未来实验中用于进一步鉴别和确认五夸克态的量子数。

Abstract: We investigate the spin parity JP assignments of experimentally observed hidden charm pentaquark states within a baryon meson molecular framework. The pentaquark mass spectrum is obtained using the Gursey Radicati mass formula, with parameters fixed through a global fit to 41 experimentally established hadron masses. The resulting spectrum is then used to assign JP quantum numbers to the observed pentaquark candidates. Within this framework, the nonstrange states Pc 4312, Pc4440, and Pc 4457 are identified with the JP = 1/2, 3/2, and 5/2 configurations, respectively. The recently reported Belle state Pcs4459, which carries strangeness, is interpreted as the strange member of the SU3 flavor octet with JP = 3/2. Magnetic moments are subsequently evaluated using explicitly constructed wave functions. Their systematic behavior across SU3 flavor multiplets and different spin parity assignments satisfies the expected sum-rule relations and indicates that magnetic moments can serve as a useful observable for refining the quantum-number identification of hidden charm pentaquark states in future studies.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The study of the Quark-Gluon Plasma (QGP), a deconfined state of nuclear matter, remains a central focus of high-energy heavy-ion collision experiments. In this study, we present comprehensive EPOS4 model predictions for key global observables in Pb-Pb collisions at $5.36$ TeV. We focus on the centrality dependence of the charged-particle pseudorapidity density ($dN_{ch}/dη$), integrated yields ($dN/dy$), mean transverse momentum ($\langle p_{T}\rangle$) for light-flavor hadrons ($π^{\pm}, K^{\pm}, p(\bar{p})$), and the charged particle nuclear modification factor ($R_{AA}$). Furthermore, the predicted charged hadron $R_{AA}$ demonstrates a clear suppression, consistent with energy loss mechanisms incorporated into the model. By comparing these predictions to existing $5.02$ TeV data, we demonstrate that the EPOS4 model offers a consistent and robust description of heavy-ion dynamics, projecting minimal energy evolution for these bulk and hard-probe observables between the two energies.

Abstract: Within the Basis Light-Front Quantization framework, we systematically investigate the subleading-twist (twist-3) generalized parton distributions (GPDs) of the proton's valence quarks beyond the Wandzura--Wilczek (WW) approximation. The twist-3 GPDs are not independent; through the equations of motion they decompose into a non-genuine contribution and a genuine twist-3 term. The latter encodes quark--quark--gluon correlations and involves interference between the light-front Fock sectors |qqq> and |qqqg>, which are typically neglected in the WW approximation. Using light-front wave functions obtained from diagonalizing the proton light-front Hamiltonian for its |qqq> and |qqqg> Fock components, we compute these GPDs via their overlap representations. Our results provide new nonperturbative input on higher-twist dynamics particularly multi-parton interference effects relevant for future measurements at the EicC and the EIC.

Motivation: 探索新型粒子如矢量类顶夸克伙伴（T）和带电Higgs玻色子在超越标准模型物理中的存在，特别是在尚未充分探测的μp对撞机环境中。

Method: 基于Type-II Two-Higgs-Doublet Model构建信号过程μ⁺p → ν_μ b̄ T → ν_μ b̄ H⁺b，其中H⁺→t b̄，进行探测器级蒙特卡洛模拟，覆盖m_H⁺≈600–650 GeV与m_T≈1.0–1.8 TeV的基准点，并评估统计显著性及系统误差鲁棒性。

Result: 在100 fb⁻¹积分亮度下，多个基准点可达>5σ发现显著性（对≤20%系统误差鲁棒）；在234 fb⁻¹下，最轻基准点显著性超10σ，且即使在30%系统误差下仍保持>5σ。

Conclusion: μp对撞机为在2HDM-II中协同探测矢量类顶伙伴与带电Higgs提供了独特且高灵敏度的平台，具备明确的发现能力。

Abstract: We investigate the discovery prospects for a vector-like top partner ($T$) within the Type-II Two-Higgs-Doublet Model (2HDM-II) at future high-energy $μp$ colliders. The analysis focuses on the charged Higgs decay mode $μ^+ p \to ν_μ\, \bar{b}T \to ν_μ\, \bar{b}H^+b$, with the subsequent decay $H^+\to t\bar{b}$ yielding a final state with multiple $b$-jets and a charged lepton. A detailed detector-level simulation is carried out for benchmark configurations with charged Higgs masses around 600-650~GeV and vector-like top masses in the range $m_T \simeq 1.0$-$1.8$~TeV. For an integrated luminosity of 100~fb$^{-1}$, discovery significances above $5σ$ are obtained across several benchmark points, remaining robust against systematic uncertainties up to 20\%. At higher luminosities of 234~fb$^{-1}$, the sensitivity exceeds $10σ$ for the lightest benchmarks and stays above $5σ$ even in the presence of 30\% systematics.

</details>

### [121] [Cosmological back-reaction of baryons on dark matter in the CAMELS simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06258)
*Matthew Gebhardt,Daniel Anglés-Alcázar,Shy Genel,Daisuke Nagai,Boon Kiat Oh,Isabel Medlock,Jonathan Mercedes-Feliz,Sagan Sutherland,Max E. Lee,Xavier Sims,Christopher C. Lovell,David N. Spergel,Romeel Davé,Matthieu Schaller,Joop Schaye,Francisco Villaescusa-Navarro*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用CAMELS项目中的数千个宇宙学流体模拟，研究了重子过程（如辐射冷却和恒星/AGN反馈）对暗物质分布的“反作用”，发现重子反馈显著改变暗物质晕的质量、密度剖面和成团性，并且该效应依赖于宇宙学参数和反馈模型细节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重子过程不仅直接重新分布重子物质，还通过引力势变化间接影响暗物质分布；为准确从弱引力透镜等观测中提取宇宙学信息，需量化并理解这种重子对暗物质的反作用。

Method: 基于CAMELS项目中SIMBA、IllustrisTNG、ASTRID和Swift-EAGLE四种星系形成模型的数千个流体模拟及其对应纯暗物质N体模拟，匹配相同晕，系统比较其质量、密度剖面与暗物质功率谱差异。

Result: 反馈导致晕的维里质量下降；中心暗物质密度因冷却而上升、外围因反馈而下降（SIMBA中中心增幅超450%）；暗物质功率谱在k~10 h/Mpc处最大可偏移±20%；该反作用同时依赖宇宙学参数（Ω_m, σ_8）和反馈模型细节。

Conclusion: 暗物质分布对重子物理高度敏感，因此在利用弱透镜等观测推断宇宙学参数时，必须对重子物理不确定性进行边缘化；同时，此类观测也具备约束星系反馈模型的潜力。

Abstract: Baryonic processes such as radiative cooling and feedback from massive stars and active galactic nuclei (AGN) directly redistribute baryons in the Universe but also indirectly redistribute dark matter due to changes in the gravitational potential. In this work, we investigate this "back-reaction" of baryons on dark matter using thousands of cosmological hydrodynamic simulations from the Cosmology and Astrophysics with MachinE Learning Simulations (CAMELS) project, including parameter variations in the SIMBA, IllustrisTNG, ASTRID, and Swift-EAGLE galaxy formation models. Matching haloes to corresponding N-body (dark matter-only) simulations, we find that virial masses decrease owing to the ejection of baryons by feedback. Relative to N-body simulations, halo profiles show an increased dark matter density in the center (due to radiative cooling) and a decrease in density farther out (due to feedback), with both effects being strongest in SIMBA (> 450% increase at r < 0.01 Rvir). The clustering of dark matter strongly responds to changes in baryonic physics, with dark matter power spectra in some simulations from each model showing as much as 20% suppression or increase in power at k ~ 10 h/Mpc relative to N-body simulations. We find that the dark matter back-reaction depends intrinsically on cosmology (Omega_m and sigma_8) at fixed baryonic physics, and varies strongly with the details of the feedback implementation. These results emphasize the need for marginalizing over uncertainties in baryonic physics to extract cosmological information from weak lensing surveys as well as their potential to constrain feedback models in galaxy evolution.

</details>


### [122] [Exploring the internal structure of a neutron star and the associated magnetic fields aided by the mass-radius relationship](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06380)
*Abriana Lyda,Prajwal MohanMurthy*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个分段模型来描述中子星的结构，特别关注地壳-核心过渡区域，并利用该模型推导出转动惯量、地壳质量分数和参与磁矩的有效中子数；结果表明毫秒脉冲星的观测磁场可完全由地壳中子极化维持，仅需约5.5%的地壳中子对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星具有远超实验室条件的磁场和密度，是研究极端条件下强相互作用物质的理想天然探针；需建立能准确刻画地壳-核心过渡（尤其是核意面区）的结构模型。

Method: 基于观测约束的质量-半径关系和符合已知状态方程的密度分布，构建一个显式包含中子滴线、核饱和密度、电子主导晕层及地壳-核心界面的分段结构模型。

Result: 模型成功再现文献报道的核意面区刚度与曲率行为；由此导出更新的转动惯量、地壳质量分数和有效磁矩中子数；发现毫秒脉冲星磁场可由地壳中子极化完全解释，仅需约≤5.5%（99%置信水平）的地壳中子对齐。

Conclusion: 支持非磁星中子星的磁场起源于地壳的物理图像，与磁热演化研究一致，并为连接中子星观测量与其内部结构提供了定量框架。

Abstract: Neutron stars exhibit magnetic fields and densities far beyond those achievable in terrestrial laboratories, offering a natural probe of strongly interacting matter under extreme conditions. Using observationally anchored mass-radius relations and a density profile consistent with established equations of state, we construct a piecewise model that explicitly integrates the neutron-drip line, nuclear-saturation, the electron-dominated halo, and core-crust interfaces. The resulting structure reproduces the stiffness and curvature behavior across the nuclear-pasta regime reported in the literature, validating our treatment of the crust-core transition. From this model, we derive updated moments of inertia, crustal mass fractions, and the effective number of neutrons contributing to the star's magnetic moment. Comparing these quantities with spin-down inferred magnetic dipole moments indicates that the observed magnetic fields of particularly millisecond pulsars can be sustained entirely by the crustal neutron polarization, requiring alignment of only about $\lesssim5.5\%$ ($99\%$ C.L.) of the neutrons in the crust. This finding supports a crust-confined magnetic-field origin for non-magnetar neutron stars, consistent with magneto-thermal evolution studies, and provides a quantitative framework for connecting neutron-star observables to its underlying structure.

### [123] [Constraining Inflation Models with Spinning Voids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06589)
*Geonwoo Kang,Jounghun Lee*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用空洞星系相干旋转引起的红移不对称性来独立、严格约束原初密度扰动标量谱指数跑动的新诊断方法，并发现该方法对非零跑动敏感，可用于检验暴胀机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非标准暴胀模型通常预言标量谱指数存在非零跑动，而现有观测手段对其约束较弱，亟需新的独立诊断方法。

Method: 利用AbacusSummit宇宙学模拟数值结果，构建空洞星系红移不对称分布的非参数模型，并分析其在不同宇宙学模型（含动态暗能量和不同初条件ΛCDM）下的普适性及其对标量谱指数跑动的响应。

Result: 发现该红移不对称模型在绝大多数宇宙学模型下高度普适，但当标量谱指数跑动偏离零时普适性被打破：正（负）跑动导致观测红移不对称性低于（高于）模型预测。

Conclusion: 空洞星系红移不对称性是一种可观测性强、对标量谱指数跑动敏感的新探针，为揭示真实暴胀机制提供了新途径。

Abstract: We present a powerful new diagnostics by which the running of scalar spectral index of primordial density fluctuations can be tightly and independently constrained. This new diagnostics utilizes coherent rotation of void galaxies, which can be observed as redshift asymmetry in opposite sides dichotomized by the projected spin axes of hosting voids. Comparing the numerical results from the AbacusSummit of cosmological simulations, we derive a non-parametric model for the redshift asymmetry distribution of void galaxies, which turns out to be almost universally valid for a very broad range of cosmologies including dynamic dark energy models with time-dependent equation of states as well as the $Λ$CDM models with various initial conditions. We discover that the universality of this model breaks down only if the running of scalar spectral index deviates from zero, detecting a consistent trend that a more positive (negative) running yields a lower (higher) redshift asymmetry of voids than the model predictions. Given that non-standard inflations usually predict non-zero runnings of the spectral index and that the redshift asymmetry distribution of voids is a readily observable quantity, we conclude that this new diagnostics will pave another path toward understanding the true mechanism of inflation.

</details>


### [124] [Impact of a negative cosmological constant on the reconstruction of dark energy in light of DESI BAO data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.06656)
*Hao Wang,Yun-Song Piao*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨负宇宙学常数（NCC）与演化暗能量组分共存的可能性，利用红移分箱和高斯过程两种方法重建暗能量状态方程w(z)，发现NCC在两种方法下均略受偏好（约1σ），且其与w(z)的简并性使w=-1的幽灵边界更符合1σ后验分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最新DESI观测暗示可能存在负宇宙学常数（NCC）真空与低红移演化正暗能量共存的情形，需探究NCC对暗能量状态方程w(z)重建的影响。

Method: 采用红移分箱（redshift-binned）和基于高斯过程（Gaussian Process-based）的两种非参数重建方法，分析NCC对演化暗能量状态方程w(z)的影响。

Result: 两种重建方法均显示NCC略受偏好（≈1σ）；NCC与w(z)存在简并性，虽削弱w(z)约束精度，却使w=-1的幽灵划分更符合1σ后验分布。

Conclusion: 负宇宙学常数可能与演化暗能量共存，其引入虽增加参数简并，但改善了w(z)在幽灵边界附近的统计一致性，支持进一步考虑NCC作为暗能量模型的组成部分。

Abstract: An anti-de Sitter vacuum, corresponding to a negative cosmological constant (NCC), might coexist with one evolving positive dark energy component at low redshift and is hinted by the latest DESI observations. In this paper, we use two methods, \textit{redshift-binned} and \textit{Gaussian Process-based} reconstructions to investigate the effect of a NCC on the equation of state (EOS) $w(z)$ of evolving dark energy (DE) component. We find that a NCC is slightly preferred in both the two reconstructions by up to $\simeq1σ$. Although the degeneracy between the EOS of evolving DE component and NCC weakens the constraint on the reconstructed $w(z)$, this degeneracy leads to the phantom divide $w=-1$ more consistent with the 1$σ$ posterior of $w(z)$.

### [125] [A New Consistency Test for the $Λ$CDM Model using Radial and Transverse BAO Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07075)
*Xing-Han A. Zhao,Zheng Cai*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需校准的、基于BAO距离测量的空间平坦ΛCDM模型一致性检验方法，通过构造BAO距离比值消除声学视界尺度，并将比值映射为有效物质密度参数Ω_M^L，验证其在红移和不同比值下是否恒定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验空间平坦ΛCDM模型的内部一致性，避免依赖于对声学视界尺度（如r_d）的校准，从而降低系统误差影响。

Method: 构造Hubble距离D_H(z)、共动角直径距离D_M(z)与体积平均距离D_V(z)之间的比值，使声学视界尺度r_d消去；将每个比值映射为等效的平坦ΛCDM物质密度参数Ω_M^L；利用积分中值定理定义涉及D_M和D_V的比值所对应的等效红移区间；应用DESI DR1与DR2的BAO数据及完整协方差矩阵进行分析。

Result: 在当前观测精度下，不同红移、不同距离比值推得的Ω_M^L值基本一致，支持平坦ΛCDM模型的内部自洽性。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种不依赖r_d校准的ΛCDM模型稳健检验手段，未来随BAO测量精度提升，其约束能力可进一步增强。

Abstract: We present a calibration-free consistency test of spatially flat $Λ$CDM based on baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) distance measurements. The method forms ratios of BAO distances -- the Hubble distance $Ð(z)$, the comoving angular diameter distance $\DM(z)$, and the volume-averaged distance $\DV(z)$ -- so that the sound horizon scale cancels, and then maps each observed ratio to an effective flat-$Λ$CDM matter density parameter, $\OmL$, defined as the value of $Ω_{\rm M}$ that reproduces the measured ratio within $Λ$CDM. Flat $Λ$CDM predicts that $\OmL$ should be independent of redshift and of the particular ratio used. For ratios involving the integrated distances $\DM$ and $\DV$, we associate them with well-defined effective line-of-sight redshift intervals using a redshift-matching strategy based on the integral mean value theorem. We apply the test to BAO measurements from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) Data Release~1 and Data Release~2, propagating the full published BAO covariance matrices into all derived ratios and $\OmL$ constraints. Within current uncertainties, the inferred $\OmL$ values are broadly consistent with a redshift-independent constant, providing an internal consistency check of flat $Λ$CDM that can be strengthened straightforwardly as BAO measurements improve.

</details>


### [126] [More power on large scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07106)
*Jeremy Mould*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了原初黑洞（PBHs）作为暗物质候选者对宇宙学模型的影响，指出其早期引力聚类可增大星系整体流速度，并通过霍金辐射导致的质量损失缓解哈勃张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释宇宙微波背景偶极矩的高值，探索暗物质可能为宏观尺度（如原初黑洞）而非基本粒子的可能性，并缓解标准ΛCDM模型中的哈勃张力问题。

Method: 采用N体模拟，从极高红移（z > 100，甚至早于辐射-物质相等时期）开始，纳入具有霍金辐射质量损失效应的PBHs，并修正弗里德曼方程中的物质密度参数Ω_m'以反映动态辐射贡献。

Result: PBH主导的早期结构形成导致更大、更长程的星系整体流速度；PBH霍金蒸发引入时变Ω_m'，等效增强早期辐射密度，减小再复合时期声视界，从而缓解哈勃常数观测值与CMB推断值之间的张力；同时影响低红移状态方程参数w的拟合。

Conclusion: PBH作为暗物质成分具有可观测宇宙学效应，尤其在大尺度流与哈勃张力方面；需在成熟宇宙学代码中进一步建模含质量损失的PBH并尽可能提前起始演化。

Abstract: The high value of the cosmic microwave dipole may be telling us that dark matter is macroscopic rather than a fundamental particle. The possible presence of a significant dark matter component in the form of primordial black holes suggests that dark halo formation simulations should be commenced well before redshift z = 100. Unlike standard CDM candidates, PBHs behave as dense, non-relativistic matter from their inception in the radiation-dominated era. This allows them to seed gravitational potential wells and begin clustering earlier. We find that starting N-body simulations at redshifts even before matter-radiation equality yield galaxy bulk flow velocities that are systematically larger than those predicted by standard LCDM models. The early, high-mass concentrations established by PBHs lead to a more rapid and efficient gravitational acceleration of surrounding baryonic and dark matter, generating larger peculiar velocities that remain coherent over scales of hundreds of Mpc. Furthermore, a sub- population of PBHs in the 10^-20 to 10^-17 solar mass range would lose a non-negligible fraction of their mass via Hawking radiation over cosmological timescales. This evaporation process converts matter into radiation, so a time-varying matter density parameter, Omega_m', is introduced, which behaves like a boosted radiation term in the Friedmann equation. This dynamic term acts to reduce the Hubble tension. A higher effective Omega_r in the early universe reduces the sound horizon at the epoch of recombination. PBH mass loss also influences fits to the equation of state parameter, w, at low redshift. The naive N-body modelling presented here suggests investigation with tried and tested cosmology codes should be carried out, by introducing mass losing PBHs and starting the evolution as early as practicable.

</details>

*Ze-fan Wang,Lei Lei,Yi-zhong Fan*

Method: 采用BAGPIPES代码对DESI发布的四千多个大质量、被动演化星系进行全谱拟合，从而获得宇宙学无关的恒星年龄与恒星形成历史，并据此推导H(z)。

Abstract: The Hubble parameter ($H(z)$) is a function of the redshift and a reliable measurement is very important to understand the expansion history of the Universe. ### [128] [Strong Evidence for Dark Sector Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07361)
*Tian-Nuo Li,William Giarè,Guo-Hong Du,Yun-He Li,Eleonora Di Valentino,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出暗物质与暗能量相互作用（IDE）模型可更好解释DESI观测到的偏离ΛCDM的BAO数据，无需引入动力学暗能量，且在参数数量相同下拟合效果优于CPL模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DESI的BAO数据显示出对ΛCDM的偏离，传统上归因于动力学暗能量，但作者试图探索是否可用更物理的暗物质-暗能量相互作用来解释。

Method: 在统一框架下，结合最新CMB（Planck/ACT/SPT）、DESI BAO和SN（含DES-Dovekie重校准）数据，分析两类IDE模型（耦合精质与耦合流体）并进行贝叶斯统计推断。

Result: 两类IDE模型均在3–5σ置信水平显示非零相互作用证据，其边缘化约束显著偏离ΛCDM极限；即使在削弱动力学DE信号的DES-Dovekie重校准后，IDE仍具优势；且拟合优度不逊于甚至优于同参数数的CPL模型。

Conclusion: IDE是动力学暗能量之外一个物理动机更强、统计支持更稳健的替代理论，亟需未来弱引力透镜、星系成团等扰动观测进一步区分二者。

Abstract: Recent DESI baryon acoustic oscillation data reveal deviations from $Λ$CDM cosmology, conventionally attributed to dynamical dark energy (DE). We demonstrate that these deviations are equally, if not better, explained by interactions between dark matter and dark energy (IDE), without requiring a time-varying DE equation of state. Using a unified framework, we analyze two IDE models--coupled quintessence and coupled fluid--against the latest CMB (Planck, ACT, SPT), DESI BAO, and SN (including DES-Dovekie recalibrated) data. Both IDE scenarios show robust evidence for non-vanishing interactions at the 3-5$σ$ level, with marginalized constraints significantly deviating from the $Λ$CDM limit. This preference persists even under DES-Dovekie SN recalibration, which weakens dynamical DE evidence. Crucially, for the same number of free parameters, IDE models provide fits to low- and high-redshift data that match or exceed the performance of the CPL dynamical DE parametrization. Our results establish IDE as a physically motivated alternative to dynamical DE, highlighting the necessity of future cosmological perturbation measurements (e.g., weak lensing, galaxy clustering) to distinguish between these paradigms.

### [129] [Modified Gravity and the Origin of the Excess Radio Galaxy Number-Count Dipole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07487)
*John. W. Moffat*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了标量-张量-矢量引力理论（STVG-MOG）是否能解释射电星系计数偶极矩超出ΛCDM预期的现象，发现该理论可在不违反其他观测约束的前提下，在超大尺度上增强引力响应，从而合理解释该异常。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期宽视场射电星系巡天观测发现宇宙计数偶极矩显著超出ΛCDM模型纯运动学预期（达3–4倍，最高5.4σ），亟需探索ΛCDM之外的物理解释。

Method: 分析STVG-MOG理论中尺度与时间依赖的有效引力耦合特性，评估其在超大尺度（Gpc）增强结构各向异性及引力响应的能力，并检验其与CMB偶极、星系动力学、弱引力透镜及晚期物质功率谱等观测的一致性。

Result: STVG-MOG可在早期宇宙和中小尺度保持标准演化，同时在Gpc尺度选择性增强引力效应，提升射电计数偶极的结构贡献而不破坏小尺度功率谱，从而一致解释观测异常。

Conclusion: 若该偶极异常确为真实宇宙信号而非系统误差，则STVG-MOG是一种可行且可检验的替代理论；射电偶极为检验最大可观测尺度上的引力物理提供了新探针。

Abstract: Recent analyses of wide-area radio-galaxy surveys have reported a statistically significant excess in the cosmic number-count dipole, with an amplitude exceeding the purely kinematic expectation of the standard $Λ$CDM model by a factor of $\sim 3$--$4$, quoted at a significance level of up to $5.4σ$. While residual observational systematics and local-structure effects cannot be definitively excluded, this result motivates the exploration of alternative physical interpretations beyond the minimal $Λ$CDM framework. We investigate whether Scalar--Tensor--Vector Gravity (STVG-MOG) can provide a consistent explanation for an enhanced large-scale anisotropic dipole without violating existing constraints from early-universe cosmology, the cosmic microwave background (CMB) dipole, galaxy dynamics, weak lensing, or the observed late-time matter power spectrum. The radio number-count dipole probes ultra-large-scale, anisotropic structure and coherent gravitational response, rather than virialized dynamics or linear growth alone. In STVG-MOG, a scale- and time-dependent effective gravitational coupling preserves standard cosmological evolution at early times and on small to intermediate scales, while amplifying gravitational response on gigaparsec scales. This scale-selective enhancement can increase the large-scale structure contribution to the radio dipole without overproducing power on smaller scales. If the observed dipole excess reflects a physical cosmological signal rather than residual systematics, STVG-MOG offers a viable and testable alternative interpretation. It is demonstrated that the radio dipole anomaly provides a novel probe of gravitational physics on the largest observable scales.

### [130] [CHEX-MATE: Relationship between X-ray and millimetre inferences of galaxy cluster temperature profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07653)
*F. De Luca,H. Bourdin,P. Mazzotta,G. Luzzi,M. G. Campitiello,M. De Petris,D. Eckert,S. Ettori,A. Ferragamo,W. Forman,M. Gaspari,F. Gastaldello,S. Ghizzardi,M. Gitti,S. T. Kay,J. Kim,L. Lovisari,J. Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过联合XMM-Newton和Planck数据，对116个CHEX-MATE星系团进行分析，测量X射线温度与SZ效应导出温度之比η_T，发现其均值为1.01±0.03，并受相对论修正和银河系分子氢吸收影响；η_T的离散主要由星系团形态决定，松弛系统更接近1且离散更小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: X射线与毫米波观测推断的星系团热力学轮廓常基于光滑球对称假设，该简化会引入系统偏差，可用于研究星系团结构或宇宙学参数。

Method: 联合XMM-Newton（X射线）与Planck（SZ效应）数据，对116个CHEX-MATE星系团分析，计算η_T = T_X / T_SZ,X；考虑SZ信号的相对论修正及银河系H2吸收；按形态分类（松弛/混合/扰动）统计η_T分布。

Result: η_T均值为1.01±0.03；忽略相对论修正和H2吸收分别使结果平均偏移8.1%和2.7%；η_T分布正偏，离散度主要由形态决定（松弛系统更集中、更接近1），与红移、质量、温度基本无关。

Conclusion: X射线与SZ温度的一致性良好，但系统偏差显著依赖于物理建模（如相对论效应、H2吸收）和星系团动力学状态，表明多波段交叉校准需谨慎考虑这些因素。

Abstract: Thermodynamic profiles from X-ray and millimetre observations of galaxy clusters are often compared under the simplifying assumptions of smooth, spherically symmetric intracluster medium. These approximations lead to expected discrepancies in the inferred profiles, which can provide insights about the cluster structure or cosmology. Motivated by this, we present a joint XMM-\textit{Newton} and \textit{Planck} analysis of 116 CHEX-MATE clusters to measure $η_T = T_X/T_{SZ,X}$, the ratio between spectroscopic X-ray temperatures and a temperature proxy derived from Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (SZ) pressures and X-ray densities. We considered relativistic corrections to the thermal SZ signal and implemented X-ray absorption by Galactic molecular hydrogen. The $η_T$ distribution has a mean of $1.01 \pm 0.03$, with average changes of $8.1\%$ and $2.7\%$ when relativistic corrections and molecular hydrogen absorption are not included, respectively. The $η_T$ distribution is positively skewed, with the scatter mostly affected by cluster morphology: relaxed clusters are closer to unity and less scattered than mixed and disturbed systems. We find little or no correlation with redshift, mass, or temperature.

### [131] [Tachyonic gravitational dark matter production after inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07670)
*Giorgio Laverda,Tomás Mendes,Javier Rubio*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由曲率诱导的不稳定驱动的暗物质非热产生新引力机制，通过标量场与时空曲率不变量（如Gauss-Bonnet）的二次耦合，在暴胀结束时引发短暂对称性破缺与粒子爆发式产生，并结合解析估计与非线性格点模拟，成功复现观测暗物质丰度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决暗物质非热产生机制中对非最小引力耦合依赖过强的问题，探索仅由时空曲率动力学驱动的、更普适且理论可控的新机制。

Method: 构建实标量场与曲率不变量（特别是Gauss-Bonnet）的二次耦合模型；利用解析方法估算不稳定性增长；开展全非线性3+1维经典格点模拟追踪系统非平衡演化；计算最终暗物质丰度并拟合通用公式。

Result: 该纯引力机制可在宽质量范围和暴胀能标下稳健重现观测暗物质密度，并给出可脱离格点模拟直接应用的经验拟合函数。

Conclusion: 曲率诱导的tachyonic不稳定性是一种可行且鲁棒的暗物质非热产生新途径，凸显了暴胀后时空几何快速演化在粒子生成中的关键作用。

Abstract: We propose a novel gravitational mechanism for the non-thermal production of dark matter driven by curvature-induced tachyonic instabilities after inflation. Departing from the commonly studied non-minimal couplings to gravity, our framework considers a real spectator scalar field coupled quadratically to spacetime curvature invariants. We show that the rapid reorganization of spacetime curvature at the end of inflation can dynamically render the dark matter field tachyonic, triggering a short-lived phase of spontaneous symmetry breaking and explosive particle production. As a concrete and theoretically controlled example, we focus on the Gauss-Bonnet topological invariant. By combining analytical estimates with fully non-linear $3+1$ classical lattice simulations, we track the out-of-equilibrium evolution of the system and compute the resulting dark matter abundance. We find that this purely gravitational mechanism can robustly reproduce the observed dark matter relic density over a wide range of masses and inflationary scales, providing also a simple fitting function that enables a lattice-independent application of our results.

</details>


### [132] [Induced gravitational waves - beyond linear cosmological perturbation theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07716)
*Raphael Picard*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了宇宙学扰动理论中高阶引力波（GWs）的产生机制，特别是标量-张量耦合和张量-张量耦合诱导的二阶GWs，并探讨了其紫外发散问题及三阶贡献与原初非高斯性的效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标量诱导引力波可能作为早期宇宙原初黑洞（PBHs）形成的观测信号，而PBHs需要大的密度扰动，这在某些暴胀模型中自然出现；但现有线性理论不足以描述其完整动力学，需拓展至高阶耦合效应。

Method: 在现有二阶标量诱导GW形式框架基础上，引入一线性张量扰动作为新源项，导出标量-张量与张量-张量诱导的二阶GW；进一步计算三阶诱导GW及其与原初GW的关联，并分析原初标量非高斯性对谱形的影响。

Result: 发现标量-张量诱导GW在原初张量模增强时显著，而张量-张量项可忽略；其谱在紫外极限下出现依赖于标量功率谱峰度的非物理解；三阶贡献整体压制信号但不消除该发散；非高斯性会调制标量-张量诱导GW谱。

Conclusion: 标量-张量耦合是二阶GW不可忽略的新通道，但其紫外行为揭示当前微扰框架的局限性；三阶效应与非高斯性虽具修正作用，尚不能完全解决发散问题，需更完备理论（如非微扰方法）进一步研究。

Abstract: This thesis focuses on gravitational waves (GWs) that arise beyond linear order in cosmological perturbation theory. In recent years, scalar-induced GWs have attracted significant attention because they may serve as the observational signature of primordial black holes (PBHs) formed in the early universe. The formation of PBHs requires large density perturbations, which can naturally emerge in some models of inflation. When these large density fluctuations couple, they act as a source for scalar-induced GWs at second order. In this work, we extend the existing formalism by including linear tensor fluctuations as an additional source term. This gives rise to two new classes of second-order GWs: those sourced by scalar-tensor couplings (scalar-tensor induced GWs) and those quadratic in tensor modes (tensor-tensor induced GWs). We find that the scalar-tensor contribution becomes significant if first-order tensor modes are enhanced, whilst the tensor-tensor contribution remains subdominant. Moreover, we demonstrate that the spectrum of scalar-tensor induced GWs exhibits an unphysical enhancement in the UV limit when the primordial scalar power spectrum is insufficiently peaked. To investigate whether this can be resolved, we study third-order induced GWs and their correlation with primordial GWs. We find that this new contribution suppresses the overall signal but does not cancel the unphysical enhancement. Possible explanations for this behaviour are discussed and left for future work. Finally, we explore the effect of primordial scalar non-Gaussianity on the spectrum of scalar-tensor induced GWs, building on previous results showing its impact on scalar-induced GWs.

</details>

*Eleni Bagui,Sébastien Clesse,Federico De Lillo,Alexander C. Jenkins,Mairi Sakellariadou*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA等探测器即将探测到引力波背景（GWB）的背景下，亟需区分不同物理起源（如PBH、致密双星并合、宇宙弦等）；而占空比这一时域特征尚未被充分用于源识别。

Method: 基于真实PBH双星种群模型，分别计算其对GWB贡献中的散粒噪声（shot-noise）、爆米花（popcorn）和连续（continuous）三类成分，并系统分析占空比对信号频率、持续时间和振幅的依赖关系。

Result: 明确了占空比是区分PBH GWB与其他源的关键可观测量；量化了其在不同频段和PBH质量分布下的行为特征；指出需发展专用数据分析工具来提取该量。

Conclusion: 占空比为PBH引力波背景识别与参数约束提供了新维度；该工作推动将时域统计特征纳入GWB源分解与宇宙学反演框架。

Abstract: Primordial black holes (PBHs) are possible sources of a gravitational-wave background (GWB), detectable with the next observing runs of LIGO--Virgo--KAGRA. In case of a detection, it will be crucial to distinguish the possible sources of this GWB. One under-explored possibility is to exploit the duty cycle that quantifies the number of sources present in the time domain signal, which can be very different depending on the nature and population of the sources. We compute the duty cycle for a realistic population of PBH binaries, isolating the shot-noise, popcorn and continuous contributions to the GWB. We identify the dependence of the duty cycle on the signal frequency, duration and amplitude as a crucial metric for distinguishing PBHs from other sources in the GWB and constraining PBH models. Our work motivates the development of specific analysis tools to extract these observables, in order to unlock new cosmological insights with upcoming GW data.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Euclid旗舰模拟，构建融合星系光度信息（星等、颜色）与宿主暗物质晕特性的IA模型；测量不同红移、星等和颜色星系样本的IA信号，并与NLA和TATT两种主流理论模型进行拟合对比；分析IA振幅随红移和光度的演化行为。

Result: NLA与TATT模型均可在6–7 h⁻¹ Mpc尺度上准确描述模拟中的IA信号；红星系IA振幅与观测一致；蓝星系在z>0.3时呈现非零但符合观测上限的信号；IA红移演化在z>1.1时偏离常用幂律，引入光度依赖后拟合显著改善。

Conclusion: Euclid旗舰模拟中的IA实现具有较高物理保真度，可作为将当前IA观测约束外推至Euclid类样本的重要工具，尤其强调在建模中纳入光度演化对提升高红移IA预测可靠性的重要性。

Abstract: We model intrinsic alignments (IA) in Euclid's Flagship simulation to investigate its impact on Euclid's weak lensing signal. Our IA implementation in the Flagship simulation takes into account photometric properties of galaxies as well as their dark matter host halos. We compare simulations against theory predictions, determining the parameters of two of the most widely used IA models: the Non Linear Alignment (NLA) and the Tidal Alignment and Tidal Torquing (TATT) models. We measure the amplitude of the simulated IA signal as a function of galaxy magnitude and colour in the redshift range $0.1<z<2.1$. We find that both NLA and TATT can accurately describe the IA signal in the simulation down to scales of $6$-$7 \,h^{-1}\,$Mpc. We measure alignment amplitudes for red galaxies comparable to those of the observations, with samples not used in the calibration procedure. For blue galaxies, our constraints are consistent with zero alignments in our first redshift bin $0.1 < z < 0.3$, but we detect a non-negligible signal at higher redshift, which is, however, consistent with the upper limits set by observational constraints. Additionally, several hydrodynamical simulations predict alignment for spiral galaxies, in agreement with our findings. Finally, the evolution of alignment with redshift is realistic and comparable to that determined in the observations. However, we find that the commonly adopted redshift power-law for IA fails to reproduce the simulation alignments above $z=1.1$. A significantly better agreement is obtained when a luminosity dependence is included, capturing the intrinsic luminosity evolution with redshift in magnitude-limited surveys. We conclude that the Flagship IA simulation is a useful tool for translating current IA constraints into predictions for IA contamination of Euclid-like samples.

Sanders,E. Sarpa,J. Schaye,A. Schneider,M. Schultheis,D. Sciotti,E. Sellentin,L. C. Smith,J. G. Sorce,K. Tanidis,C. Tao,G. Testera,R. Teyssier,S. Tosi,A. Troja,M. Tucci,C. Valieri,A. Venhola,D. Vergani,F. Vernizzi,G. Verza,P. Vielzeuf,N. A. Walton*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个半解析模型来预测欧几里得（Euclid）弱引力透镜观测中星系本征取向（intrinsic alignments）的污染效应，模型基于Euclid Flagship模拟，并结合COSMOS、SDSS和Horizon-AGN等多源观测与模拟数据进行校准，最终预测Euclid任务结束时的层析弱透镜两点统计量将因本征取向而改变达约10%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 星系本征取向是弱引力透镜宇宙学分析中潜在的主要系统误差来源，亟需建模并量化其影响。

Method: 基于Euclid Flagship N体模拟，构建半解析模型：星系形状与取向由其宿主暗晕性质及星系在晕内的相对位置决定；引入随机场错位机制，分别处理中心星系与卫星星系，并依赖红移、光度和静止帧颜色调节取向强度；用COSMOS椭率统计、SDSS对齐测量和Horizon-AGN在z=1处的取向数据联合校准模型。

Result: 最优拟合模型含12个对齐参数，整体在观测与模拟的1σ统计误差内较好复现校准数据，但最亮子样本在小尺度上存在明显偏差；当前校准数据统计精度和Flagship单一实现体积尚不足以对相关星系样本的本征对齐振幅提供有信息量的先验范围；预测Euclid层析弱透镜两点统计受本征取向影响最大可达~10%。

Conclusion: 该半解析模型为Euclid等下一代巡天项目提供了可校准、物理动机明确的本征对齐建模框架，但需更高统计精度的校准数据与更大体积模拟以进一步约束关键参数。

Abstract: Intrinsic alignments of galaxies are potentially a major contaminant of cosmological analyses of weak gravitational lensing. We construct a semi-analytic model of galaxy ellipticities and alignments in the \Euclid Flagship simulation to predict this contamination in Euclid's weak lensing observations. Galaxy shapes and orientations are determined by the corresponding properties of the host haloes in the underlying $N$-body simulation, as well as the relative positions of galaxies within their halo. Alignment strengths are moderated via stochastic misalignments, separately for central and satellite galaxies and conditional on the galaxy's redshift, luminosity, and rest-frame colour. The resulting model is calibrated against galaxy ellipticity statistics from the COSMOS Survey, selected alignment measurements based on Sloan Digital Sky Survey samples, and galaxy orientations extracted from the Horizon-AGN hydrodynamic simulation at redshift $z=1$. The best-fit model has a total of 12 alignment parameters and generally reproduces the calibration data sets well within the $1σ$ statistical uncertainties of the observations and the \flagship simulation, with notable exceptions for the most luminous sub-samples on small physical scales. The statistical power of the calibration data and the volume of the single \flagship realisation are still too small to provide informative prior ranges for intrinsic alignment amplitudes in relevant galaxy samples. As a first application, we predict that \Euclid end-of-mission tomographic weak gravitational lensing two-point statistics are modified by up to order $10\,\%$ due to intrinsic alignments.

</details>


### [136] [Cosmoglobe DR2. V. Spatial correlations between thermal dust and ionized carbon emission in Planck HFI and COBE-DIRBE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07818)
*E. Gjerløw,R. M. Sullivan,R. Aurvik,A. Basyrov,L. A. Bianchi,A. Bonato,M. Brilenkov,H. K. Eriksen,U. Fuskeland,M. Galloway,K. A. Glasscock,L. T. Hergt,D. Herman,J. G. S. Lunde,M. San,A. I. Silva Martins,D. Sponseller,N. -O. Stutzer,H. Thommesen,V. Vikenes,D. J. Watts,I. K. Wehus,L. Zapelli*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过拟合五种热尘埃辐射示踪剂（H i、CO、Hα、尘埃消光和C ii）到Planck和COBE-DIRBE的多频段数据，发现C ii在高于1 THz频段起主导作用，且其相关成分温度最高（约25 K）；Hα成分则表现为吸收而非发射；该简单模型在1 THz以下可解释98%的信号RMS，表明大尺度上尘埃SED的空间变化可能源于各向同性物理组分的空间混合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解不同物理环境对热尘埃辐射的相对贡献，并探究其随频率和天区位置的变化规律，以改进宇宙微波背景研究中的前景建模。

Method: 使用五种外部模板（HI4PI、Dame CO、WHAM Hα、Gaia消光、COBE-FIRAS C ii）进行多变量线性回归，联合拟合10个频段（353 GHz–25 THz）数据；所有成分均用修正黑体谱能量分布（SED）建模，并估计各自有效温度及最大贡献频率。

Result: C ii在>1 THz频段主导信号，>10 THz时几乎完全主导；C ii成分最热（~25 K），Hα为18 K且呈吸收特征；所有成分SED可用修正黑体描述，峰值频率在1–5 THz间；模型在<1 THz下解释98% RMS信号。

Conclusion: 热尘埃辐射的大尺度变化可主要由几种物理上明确、空间各向同性SED的成分混合来解释，无需引入复杂的空间变化SED参数，为前景减除提供了更简洁有效的建模思路。

Abstract: We fit five tracers of thermal dust emission to ten Planck HFI and COBE-DIRBE frequency maps between 353 GHz and 25 THz, aiming to map the relative importance of each physical host environment as a function of frequency and position on the sky. Four of these correspond to classic thermal dust tracers, namely H i (HI4PI), CO (Dame et al. 2001a), Hα (WHAM, Haffner et al. (2003a, 2016)), and dust extinction (Gaia; Edenhofer et al. 2024), while the fifth is ionized carbon (C ii) emission as observed by COBE- FIRAS. We jointly fit these five templates to each frequency channel through standard multi-variate linear regression. At frequencies higher than 1 THz, we find that the dominant tracer is in fact C ii, and above 10 THz this component accounts for almost the entire fitted signal; at frequencies below 1 THz, its importance is second only to H i. We further find that all five components are well described by a modified blackbody spectral energy density (SED) up to some component-dependent maximum frequency ranging between 1 and 5 THz. In this interpretation, the C ii-correlated component is the hottest among all five, with an effective temperature of about 25 K. The Hα component has a temperature of 18 K, and, unlike the other four, is observed in absorption rather than emission. Despite the simplicity of this model, which relies only on external templates coupled to spatially isotropic SEDs, we find that it captures 98 % of the full signal root mean squared (RMS) below 1 THz. This high efficiency suggests that spatial variations in the thermal dust SED, as for instance reported by Planck and other experiments, may be more economically modelled on large angular scales in terms of a spatial mixing of individually isotropic physical components.

</details>


### [137] [Cosmoglobe DR2. VII. Towards a concordance model of large-scale thermal dust emission for microwave and infrared frequencies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07822)
*E. Gjerløw,R. M. Sullivan,R. Aurvik,A. Basyrov,L. A. Bianchi,A. Bonato,M. Brilenkov,H. K. Eriksen,U. Fuskeland,M. Galloway,K. A. Glasscock,L. T. Hergt,D. Herman,J. G. S. Lunde,M. San,A. I. Silva Martins,D. Sponseller,N. -O. Stutzer,H. Thommesen,V. Vikenes,D. J. Watts,I. K. Wehus,L. Zapelli*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用COBE-DIRBE数据，通过贝叶斯方法拟合四组分热尘埃模型（热尘、冷尘、近邻尘、Hα相关尘），各组分采用固定空间模板与各通道自由振幅的各向同性谱能量分布（SED）建模；结果表明模型在多数波段能解释95%以上信号方差，在60/100微米达70%，且热尘成分在3.5微米占总信号80%以上，为构建微波与红外统一尘埃发射模型奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立适用于微波与红外波段的联合热尘埃发射一致模型，提升对银河系尘埃辐射物理性质的理解与建模精度。

Method: 基于Cosmoglobe DR2贝叶斯端到端重分析框架，对COBE-DIRBE 3.5–240微米数据拟合四组分热尘埃模型；每个组分由固定空间模板和每通道自由振幅定义的各向同性SED描述；共25个DIRBE专属自由度。

Result: 除冷尘振幅仅在240微米稳健探测外，其余三组分在12–240微米所有通道均显著探测；3.5/4.9微米仅热尘被探测；1.25/2.2微米受星光主导无法稳健探测；模型在低高频捕获>95%方差，60/100微米约70%；热尘在3.5微米贡献≥80%总信号，并与C ii强相关。

Conclusion: 该四组分模型成功刻画DIRBE频段尘埃辐射特征，验证其与Astrodust预测一致性，是迈向微波–红外统一尘埃模型的关键一步。

Abstract: We fit a four-component thermal dust model to COBE-DIRBE data between 3.5 and 240 micron within the global Bayesian end-to- end Cosmoglobe DR2 reanalysis. Following a companion analysis of Planck HFI, the four components of this model correspond to "hot dust", "cold dust", "nearby dust", and "Halpha correlated dust", respectively, and each component is modelled in terms of a fixed spatial template and a spatially isotropic spectral energy density (SED) defined by an overall free amplitude for each DIRBE channel. Except for the cold dust amplitude, which is only robustly detected in the 240 micron channel, we measure statistically significant template amplitudes for all components in all DIRBE channels between 12 and 240 micron. In the 3.5 and 4.9 micron channels, only the hot component is detected, while the 1.25 and 2.2 micron channels are too dominated by starlight emission to allow robust dust detections. The total number of DIRBE-specific degrees of freedom in this model is 25. Despite this low dimensionality, the resulting total SED agrees well with recent astrodust predictions. At both low and high frequencies, more than 95 % of the frequency map variance is captured by the model, while at 60 and 100 micron about 70 % of the signal variance is successfully accounted for. The hot dust component, which in a companion paper has been found to correlate strongly with C ii emission, has the highest absolute amplitude in all DIRBE frequency channels; in particular, at 3.5 micron, which is known to be dominated by polycyclic aromatic hydrocarbon emission, this component accounts for at least 80 % of the total signal. This analysis represents an important step towards establishing a joint concordance model of thermal dust emission applicable to both the microwave and infrared regimes.

</details>


### [138] [Cosmoglobe DR2. IV. Modelling starlight in DIRBE with Gaia and WISE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07831)
*M. Galloway,E. Gjerløw,M. San,R. M. Sullivan,D. J. Watts,R. Aurvik,A. Basyrov,L. A. Bianchi,A. Bonato,M. Brilenkov,H. K. Eriksen,U. Fuskeland,K. A. Glasscock,L. T. Hergt,D. Herman,J. G. S. Lunde,A. I. Silva Martins,D. Sponseller,N. -O. Stutzer,H. Thommesen,V. Vikenes,I. K. Wehus,L. Zapelli*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文基于Gaia和WISE数据构建了DIRBE在1.25–25 μm波段的恒星光发射模型，区分亮星（逐颗拟合PHOENIX SED）与暗弱源弥散背景（整体归一化），量化了恒星对各波段DIRBE观测通量的贡献（如2.2 μm占91%，25 μm仅1%），为精确提取宇宙红外背景和黄道光信号奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确分离恒星发射是精确测量宇宙红外背景（CIB）和黄道光（ZL）的前提，而DIRBE数据中恒星污染显著，需高精度建模。

Method: 结合Gaia（提供恒星物理参数与位置）与WISE（提供多波段测光）数据：对42万+亮星，用PHOENIX模型库匹配其有效SED并卷积DIRBE带通，在Cosmoglobe DR2贝叶斯框架中逐星拟合振幅；对7.1亿未入选亮星的WISE源，统一叠加为弥散背景并每波段拟合单一振幅。

Result: 恒星总辐射贡献DIRBE观测通量的91%（2.2 μm）、54%（4.9 μm）和1%（25 μm）；该模型精度足以支撑CIB单极子与黄道光在DIRBE最高三个频段的高精度分离。

Conclusion: 本工作建立了迄今最精细的DIRBE波段恒星光发射模型，通过分层处理亮星与暗源，显著提升了对非恒星红外背景成分（如CIB、ZL）的提取精度，验证了其在宇宙学与行星际尘埃研究中的关键作用。

Abstract: We present a model of starlight emission in the Diffuse Infrared Background Explorer (DIRBE) data between 1.25 and 25$\,μ$m based on \textit{Gaia} and WISE measurements. We include two classes of compact objects, namely bright stars with individual spectral energy densities (SEDs) measured by \textit{Gaia}, and a combined diffuse background of dim point source emission. Of the 424\ 829 bright sources that we fit, the number of stars with a flux density detected by WISE at Galactic latitudes $|b|>20^{\circ}$ at more than $5\,σ$ is 94\,680, for an average of 1.36~stars per DIRBE beam area. For each star, we adopt physical parameters ($T_{\mathrm{eff}}$, $\log g$, and [M/H]) from \textit{Gaia}; use these to identify a best-fit effective SED with the PHOENIX stellar model library; convolve with the respective DIRBE bandpass; and fit an overall free amplitude per star within the Bayesian end-to-end \texttt{Cosmoglobe} DR2 framework. The contributions from faint sources are accounted for by coadding all 710\ 825\ 587 WISE sources not included as bright stars, and fit one single overall amplitude per DIRBE band. Based on this model we find that total star emission accounts for 91\,\% of the observed flux density at 2.2\,$μ$m; 54\,\% at 4.9$\,μ$m; and 1\,\% at 25\,$μ$m. As shown in companion papers, this new model is sufficiently accurate to support high-precision measurements of both the Cosmic Infrared Background monopole and zodiacal light emission in the three highest DIRBE frequencies.

</details>


### [139] [Axion misalignment as a synchronization phenomenon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.07836)
*Veronica Sanz*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出将轴子失准（axion misalignment）重新解释为一种涌现的集体现象，类比于耦合振荡器系统的同步行为，指出宏观轴子相位可由初始非相干态在膨胀宇宙中通过梯度驱动而自发形成；失准角并非基本初值，而是相位相干建立后才定义的集体变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统轴子失准机制将失准角视为任意初值，导致对初始条件高度敏感和精细调节问题；本文旨在从集体动力学角度提供更自然、动力学自洽的物理解释。

Method: 建立轴子场动力学与耦合振荡器同步现象之间的明确类比，构建简单格点模型，在膨胀宇宙背景下模拟梯度驱动的相位有序化过程，并分析集体相位如何在轴子开始振荡前被选定。

Result: 证明宏观轴子相位可动态产生于初始无序态；失准角作为集体变量仅在相位相干建立后才有意义；格点模型显示集体相位在振荡 onset 前即被确定，从而为标准失准图像提供动力学基础。

Conclusion: 轴子失准应被视为一种涌现现象而非初始条件；该视角重构了对初值敏感性的理解，将人择小角度论证转化为相位有序效率问题，并暗示早期宇宙中精细调节可能普遍关联于涌现集体动力学。

Abstract: We propose a dynamical reinterpretation of axion misalignment as an emergent collective phenomenon. Drawing an explicit parallel between axion field dynamics and synchronization in coupled oscillator systems, we show that a macroscopic axion phase can arise dynamically from initially incoherent configurations through gradient-driven ordering in an expanding Universe. In this framework, the misalignment angle is not a fundamental initial condition but a collective variable that becomes well defined only once phase coherence develops. Using a simple lattice model, we illustrate how the collective phase is selected prior to the onset of axion oscillations, providing a dynamical basis for the standard misalignment picture. This perspective offers a new way of organizing axion initial-condition sensitivity, reframes anthropic small-angle arguments in terms of phase-ordering efficiency, and suggests a broader connection between fine-tuning and emergent collective dynamics in the early Universe.

</details>
